
1a1(mdo 'grel): ched du brjod pa'i tshoms dgra bcom pa chos skyobs kyis bsdus pa bzhugs so//
1b1(mdo 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ u dA na brga/ bod skad du/ ched du brjod pa'i tshems/ thams cad mkhyen
1b2(mdo 'grel): pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bkra shis par gyur cig /rgyal bas ched du brjod gsungs pa/ /bdag gis rab tu bshad
1b3(mdo 'grel): par byas/ /gnyid dang rmugs pa rnam sol la/ /yid la dga' ba bskyed de nyon/ /thams cad mkhyen pa skyob pa po/ /
1b4(mdo 'grel): thub pa chen po thugs brtse ba/ /sku yi tha ma 'dzin pa'i tshe/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad gsungs/ /kye ma 'dus
2a1(mdo 'grel): byas rnams mi rtag /skye zhing 'jig pa'i chos can yin/ /skyes nas 'jig par gyur pa ste/ /de dag myur
2a2(mdo 'grel): du zhi ba bde/ /de ltar rab tu 'bar ba la/ /ci zhig dgar yod mgur ci yod/ /mun pa'i nang zhugs gnas pa dag /ci phyir
2a3(mdo 'grel): sgron ma tshol mi byed/ /rus pa thi ba'i mdog 'dra ba/ /bor ba gang yin 'di dag ni/ /phyogs dang phyogs su rnam 'thor ba/ /
2a4(mdo 'grel): de mthong 'di la ci zhig dga' / /gang gi nub mo kho na nas/ /mngal du dang po zhugs pa'i mi/ /de ni sdod med 'gro 'gyur zhing/ /
2b1(mdo 'grel): song ba las kyang ldog pa med/ /snga dro skye bo mang mthong ba/ /phyi dro kha cig mthong mi 'gyur/ /phyi dro skye bo gang mthong ba/ /snga dro kha cig mthong mi 'gyur/ /
2b2(mdo 'grel): skyes pa bud med mang po dang/ /dar la bab pa'ang 'chi 'gyur na/ /de la mi 'di gzhon zhes te/ /gson pa'i gdengs drod ci zhig yod/ /kha cig mngal du
2b3(mdo 'grel): 'chi bar 'gyur/ /de bzhin kha cig btsas pa'i sar/ /de bzhin kha cig 'gog tsam na/ /de bzhin kha cig yongs rgyug na/ /la la rgan dang la la gzhon/
2b4(mdo 'grel): la la dar la bab pa'o mi/ /rim gyis rab tu 'gro 'gyur te/ /'bras bu smin pa ltung 'gyur bzhin/ /dper na 'bras bu smin pa rnams/ /ltung bas
2b5(mdo 'grel): rtag tu 'jig pa ltar/ /de bzhin skyes par gyur pa'i mi/ /rtag tu 'chi bas 'jig par 'gyur/ /dper na rdza ma'i mkhan pa yis/ /'jim pa las ni
3a1(mdo 'grel): snod byas pa/ /thams cad tha mar 'jig pa ltar/ /mi rnams srog kyang de bzhin no/ /dper na thags ni bskyang ba la/ /spun ni gang dang gang bcug pa'i/ /
3a2(mdo 'grel): spun gyis gting la gtugs pa ltar/ /mi rnams srog kyang de bzhin no/ /dper na nges par bsad pa dag /gom pa gang dang gang bor ba/ /bsad sa'i drung du bsnyen pa
3a3(mdo 'grel): ltar/ /mi rnams srog kyang de bzhin no/ /chu klung drag tu 'bab pa'i rgyun/ /ldog pa med pa ji lta bar/ /de bzhin mi yi tshe 'gro ba/ /slar ni ldog par 'gyur ba med/ /
3a4(mdo 'grel): dka' ba nyid dang thung ba dang/ /de yang sdug bsngal ldan pa dag /myur ba kho nar 'jig 'gyur te/ /chu la dbyu gus bris pa bzhin/ /dper na phyugs rdzi dbyug thogs kyis//
3a5(mdo 'grel): phyugs rnams gnas su phyin byed ltar/ /de bzhin nad dang rga ba yis/ /mi rnams 'chi bdag drung du skyel/ /chu bran gyi ni chu lta bu/ /nyin dang mtshan mo 'das pa yis/ /mi
3b1(mdo 'grel): rnams tshe yang zad 'gyur zhing/ /srog kyang nye bar 'jig par 'gyur/ /mel tshe byed la mtshan mo ring/ /lam gyis dub la rgyang grags ring/ /dam chos rnam par mi shes pa'i/ /byis pa rnams la 'khor
3b2(mdo 'grel): ba ring/ /bdag la bu yod de bzhin du/ /nor yod ces pas byis pa brlag /phyi rol nang na bdag med na/ /su yi bu yin ci zhig nor/ /skyes pa bud med rnams kyi rigs/ /brgya dang stong phrag mang po
3b3(mdo 'grel): dang/ /longs spyod legs par bsgrubs pa yang/ /'chi bdag dbang du 'gro bar 'gyur/ /bsags pa kun gyi mdza' zad cing/ /bslang ba'i mdza' ni 'gyol bar 'gyur/ /phrad pa'i mdza' ni 'bral ba
3b4(mdo 'grel): ste/ /gson pa'i mdza' ni 'chi ba yin/ /gson mdza' 'chi ba yin pas na/ /sems can thams cad 'chi 'gyur zhing/ /dge sdig 'bras bu nyer 'gro ba'i/ /ji bzhi las kyi rjes su 'breng/ /srig
3b5(mdo 'grel): pa'i las kyis dmyal ba dang/ /bsod nams byas pas bde 'gro ste/ /gzhan dag gis ni lam bsgoms pas/ /zag med mya ngan las par 'gyur/ /gang yang sangs rgyas rang sangs rgyas/ /sangs
3b6(mdo 'grel): rgyas rnams kyi nyan thos kyang/ /sku lus 'di ni spong mdzad na/ /skye bo phal pa smos ci dgos/ /gang du gnas na 'chi bas mi tshugs pa'i/ /sa phyogs de ni yod pa ma yin te/ /bar snang la med rgya mtsho'i
4a1(mdo 'grel): nang na med/ /ri bo rnams kyi gseb tu zhugs na'ang min/ /byung dang 'byung bar 'gyur ba ji snyed pa/ /kun gyi lus 'di btang nas 'gro ba dang/ /de kun 'jig par mkhas pas
4a2(mdo 'grel): rtogs bgyis te/ /chos la gnas pas nges par spyad pa spyod/ /rga ba mthong zhing nad kyi sdug bsngal dang/ /sems bral ba yi shi ba mthong nas ni/ /ston pas btson ra 'dra ba'i khyim spangs kyi/ /'jig rten
4a3(mdo 'grel): phal pas 'dod spong nus re skan/ /rgyal po'i shing rta shin tu bkra ba'ang 'jig /de bzhin lus kyang nye bar rga bar 'gyur/ /dam pa rnams kyi chos 'di dam pa ste/ /mi mchog gzhan
4a4(mdo 'grel): rtogs byed cing rgas mi 'gyur/ /rga ba khyod ni kun zhing ngan/ /khyod ni mi rigs byed pa ste/ /yid du 'ong ba'i gzugs 'di yang/ /khyod kyis mngon par bcom par 'gyur/ /gang zhig
4a5(mdo 'grel): lo ni brgyar 'tshe ba/ /de yang 'chi bdag nyid kyis khrid/ /'di dag rga bar 'gyur ba 'am/ /yang na na ba 'am 'chi bas 'joms/ /rtag tu ldog pa med par 'gro 'gyur zhing/ /
4a6(mdo 'grel): nyin dang mtshan du rab tu 'jig pa dang/ /skye dang 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal dang ldan pa/ /chu tshan nang du 'dus pa'i nya dang 'dra/ /tshe 'di nyin dang mtshan mo dang/ /'gro
4b1(mdo 'grel): ba dang ni 'dug pa na/ /chu klung chen po'i rgyun bzhin du/ /phyir mi ldog par 'gro bar 'gyur/ /chu chung nang gi nya lta bu/ /gang zhig nyin zhag 'das sa yis/ /tshe 'di shin tu thung 'gyur na/ /de la dga' bar bya ci yod/ /gson mdza' 'chi
4b2(mdo 'grel): pa yin pa'i phyir/ /lus 'di yongs su rga ba dang/ /nad kyi tshang 'di myur 'jig cing/ brnag gi chogs kyang 'jig par 'gyur/ /kye ma lus 'di mi thogs par/ /gtong zhing rnam shes dang bral nas/ /dur khrod bor ba'i mgal du ma ltar/
4b3(mdo 'grel): sa yi steng du 'gyel bar 'gyur/ /rgyun du nad kyis mngon gdungs shing/ /rtag tu mi gtsang 'dzag pa dang/ /rga dang 'chi ba'i tshor 'grib pa'i/ /lus 'di de ma cir mi rung/ /myur du 'jig cing na ba dang/ /rnag dang ldan pa'i lus 'di
4b4(mdo 'grel): yis/ /grub dang bde ba bla med pa/ /zhi mchog don du gnyer bar gyis/ /dgun ka dang ni dpyid ka dang/ /dbyar ka 'di dag bya'o zhes/ /byis pa rnam par sems byed pas/ /bar chad mthong bar ma gyur to/ /bu dang nor phyugs 'byor ba la/ /mi
4b5(mdo 'grel): yi yid ni rnam chags pa/ /'chi bdag gis ni blangs nas 'gro/ /nyal grong chu bos 'das pa bzhin/ 'chi ba'i dus la bab pa na/ /bu rnams skyabs su mi 'gyur zhing/ /pha yang ma yin gnyen 'dun min/ /khyod la skyabs su 'gyur
4b6(mdo 'grel): pa med/ /'di ni bya ba byas zin don 'di bya/ /de dag byas nas bdag gis 'di bya'o zhes/ /de ltar mi 'di yongs su shom pa na/ /rga dang nad bcas 'chi bas mngon du bcom/ /de ltar rtag tu ting 'dzin la dga' mnyam pa zhog /brtson
4b7(mdo 'grel): pa bskyed la skye dang rga ba'i mdza' ma ltos/ /bdud rnams sde dang bcas pa mngon par zil non la/ /dge slong dag gis skye shi pha rol 'gro bar gyis/ /mi rtag pa'i tshoms te dang po'o// //kun rtog las ni 'dod skyes pas/ /'dod pa'i
5a1(mdo 'grel): rtsa bar shes bgyis te/ /khyod ni kun rtog mi byed dang/ /des na khyod la 'byung mi 'gyur/ /'dod pa rnams las mya ngan skye/ /'dod pa rnams las 'jigs pa 'byung/ /'dod pa dag ni rnam spangs na/ /mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa
5a2(mdo 'grel): med/ /dga' ba rnams las mya ngan skye/ /dga' ba rnams las 'jigs pa 'byung/ /dga' ba dag ni rnams spangs na/ /mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa med/ /'dod dga' i rnam smin sdug bsngal te/ /dang po mngar la 'bras bu tsha/ /me sgron
5a3(mdo 'grel): lag nas ma bor ba/ /mjug tu byis pa sreg byed bzhin/ /nor bu rna cha bu dang bu mo la/ /yongs su chags sems gang yin la bltos na/ /lcags shing gres ma la byas chings ma gang/ /de dag dam po min zhes 'phags pa gsung/
5a4(mdo 'grel): 'dod pa'i 'chings ma gang yin de lhod kyang/ /rab tu dgrol bar dka' zhes 'phags pa gsung/ /brtan rnams 'dod pa'i bde la mi lta bar/ /de dag gtubs nas myur du 'gro bar byed/ /'jig rten sna tshogs gang de 'dod min gyi/ /skyes
5a5(mdo 'grel): bu'i kun rtog 'dod chags 'dod pa yin/ /'jig rten sna tshogs de bzhin gnas kyang ni/ /'on kyang brtan rnams 'di la 'dun pa 'dul/ /mi rnams la ni rtag pa'i 'dod pa med/ /'dod can gang la chags de mi rtag pas/ /yang srid
5a6(mdo 'grel): med phyir sems kyis rab spongs la/ /'chi ba'i gnas mi 'gyur par byos zhes gsungs/ /'dun pa skyes shing zag pa mi byed dang/ /sems la skyon med pa dang dran pa dang/ /'dod pa rnams la so sor ma chags gang/ /de ni gong du 'pho ba yin
5a7(mdo 'grel): zhes gsungs/ /mgar ba yis ni rdul bzhin du/ /blo gros ldan pas rim pa bzhin/ /skad cig skad cig cung zad tsam/ /rang gi dri ma bsal bar bya/ /lham mkhan gyis ni ko ba dag /yongs su sbyangs nas lham byed ltar/ /'dod pa gang dang gang
5b1(mdo 'grel): spangs pa/ /de de bde ba phun sum ldan/ /gal te bde ba kun 'dod na/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs su spongs/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs spangs pas/ /mchog tu bde ba thob par 'gyur/ /ji srid 'dod pa'i rjes 'breng ba/ /de srid par du ngoms
5b2(mdo 'grel): mi 'gyur/ /de la gang dag shes rab kyis/ /ldog byed de dag tshim pa thob/ /'dod pas ngoms par mi 'gyur bas/ /shes rab kyis ni ngoms pa bskyed/ /shes rab kyis ni ngoms pa'i mi/ /srid pa'i dbang du mi 'gyur ro/ /'dod la chags
5b3(mdo 'grel): pa'i mi gang yin/ /de dag kye ma chos min dga' / /cung zad gson par 'dug pa na/ /bar chad mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/ /blo ngan longs spyod kyis bcom pa/ /pha rol tshol bar mi byed cing/ /bsam brlag 'dod la sred pa yis/ /bdag
5b4(mdo 'grel): dang gzhan yang phung bar byed/ /karSha pa ne'i char bab kyang/ /'dod pa rnams kyis ngoms mi 'gyur/ /'dod pa mnog chung nyes mang bar/ /mkhas pa rnams kyis khong du chud/ /lha yid 'dod pa rnams la yang/ /lhag par dga' bar
5b5(mdo 'grel): mi 'gyur gyi/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas dang nyan thos rnams/ /sred pa zad pas dgyes par 'gyur/ /gangs can dang ni mnyam pa yi/ /gser gyi ri bo yod gyur kyang/ /nor des gcig kyang mi tshim par/ /rtogs par gyis la legs
5b6(mdo 'grel): par spyod/ /gang dag sdug bsngal de yi rgyur shes pa/ /de dag nam yang 'dod la dga' mi 'gyur/ /'jig rten dag na zug rngu'i rgyur shes nas/ /de dag gdul phyir brtan pa slob par byed/ /'dod pa'i tshoms te gnyis pa'o// //
5b7(mdo 'grel): lus can rnam par rtog pas rab bcom nas/ /'dod chags mi bzad gtsang mar rjes lta bas/ /'dod chags phyir zhing rab tu 'phel 'gyur te/ /rang gi 'ching ba de yis dam por byed/ /gang dag rnam rtog nye bar zhi dga' zhing/ /
6a1(mdo 'grel): mi sdug bsgom pa rtag tu dran byed de/ /de yis srid pa rab tu spangs pa yis/ /rang gi 'ching ba de dag 'dul bar byed/ /'dod pa mun nag dra bas g.yogs/ /sred pa'i dga' ? pas bkab pa dang/ /bag med 'ching
6a2(mdo 'grel): bas bcings pa dag /ched mar chud pa'i nya dang 'dra/ /skyes bu bag med rab tu spyod byed pa/ /'khri shing bzhin du sred pa 'phel 'gyur zhing/ /rga dang 'chi ba'i rjes su 'gro 'gyur te/ /ma drung nu zho 'dod pa'i be'u dang 'dra/ /
6a3(mdo 'grel): mi dag dran par byed dang chags byed dang/ /yid bde ba la rtog par byed pa dag /de yis yang dang yang du 'khor par 'khyam/ /tshal nang 'bras bu 'dod pa'i spre'u dang mtshungs/ /mi gang rtag tu bde bar 'dod byed pa/ /skye dang rga
6a4(mdo 'grel): bar nye bar 'gro 'gyur zhing/ /bdud kyi sbyor ba dag dang ldan pa de/ /rga dang 'chi ba'i rjes su 'gro 'gyur te/ /skye dgu sred pa rnams kyis mdun du bdar/ /rgya nang ri bong yongs su rgyug pa bzhin/ /sred pa rnams kyis mdud pa'i sems
6a5(mdo 'grel): can dag /srid dang srid min dag la sems chags shing/ /kun sbyong rol dga' ba'i sems can rnams/ /yang dang yang du sdug bsngal thob par 'gyur/ /skye bo grub dang bde ba dang bral zhing/ /bdud kyi sbyor ba dag dang ldan pa de/ /rga dang
6a6(mdo 'grel): 'chi ba'i rjes su 'gro 'gyur te/ /ma drung nu zho 'dod pa'i be'u dang 'dra/ /'di na sred pa de 'dra spong byed pa/ /srid dang srid min dag la sred bral zhing/ /dge slong srid pa zil gyis gnon byed pa/ /lhag ma med par yongs su mya ngan 'da' / /gang
6a7(mdo 'grel): zhig 'jig rten spang dka' ba'i/ /srid pa'i bud med 'dis 'khol ba/ /de yi mya ngan 'phel 'gyur te/ /rtsa la char pa bab pa bzhin/ /gang zhig 'jig rten spang dka' ba'i/ /sred pa'i bud med 'di spong ba/ /de yi mya ngan ldog 'gyur te//
6b1(mdo 'grel): pad+ma las ni chu thigs bzhin/ /de phyir ji snyed 'dir lhags? pa/ /khyed la smra yis khyed bde shog /u shir phyir ni rtswa bzhin du/ /sred pa rtswar bcas drungs nas phyung/ /skyes bu sred pa dang 'grogs na/ /yun rings dus su 'khyam 'gyur bas/ /sred pa
6b2(mdo 'grel): drungs nas phyung zhig dang/ /mya ngan med cing 'jigs ma byed/ /yang dang yang du nyer len cing/ /yang dang yang du mngal du 'jug /gnas skabs 'gyur dang gzhan 'gyur bas/ /sems can 'od dang 'gro bar byed/ /'dir ni spang dka' i sred
6b3(mdo 'grel): pa de/ /spongs la sa bon chod cig dang/ /de la sred pa med 'gyur zhing/ /de ni yang du 'khor mi 'gyur/ /dal 'byor chud 'di ma gsan par/ /gang gis lha dang mi rnams su/ /don gnyer bcings nas 'jog byed pa/ /yul la sred pa de nas
6b4(mdo 'grel): rgol/ /sems can dmyal bar skyes na yang/ /dal 'byor thal bas 'gyod par 'ong/ /gang tshe srid mtsho'i rgyur gyur pa/ /yul la sred pa 'bras kyi gzhi/ /'khri shing dra bas khebs byed pa/ /gdung bar byed pa ma btul na/ /sdug bsngal 'di
6b5(mdo 'grel): ni yang dang yang/ /rnam pa kun tu ldog mi 'gyur/ /dper na ljon shing rtsad nas ma gton na/ /bcad kyang phyir zhing skye ba kho nar zad/ /de bzhin sred pa'i phra rgyas ma gton na/ /yang dang yang du sdug bsngal 'di mi ldog /dper na bdag nyid
6b6(mdo 'grel): kyis ni byas pa'i mtshon/ /de yis rkun po'i mthu yid bdag gsod ltar/ /de bzhin nang gi sems las byung ba yi/ /sred pas lus can nye bar gsod par byed/ /de ltar sred las sdug bsngal dag /'byung ba'i nyes dmigs shes bgyis te//
6b7(mdo 'grel): srod spongs nye bar len med dang/ /dran ldan dge slong kun tu rgyus/ /sred pa'i tshoms te gsum pa'o// //bag yod mchi med gnas yin te/ /bag med pa ni 'chi ba'i gnas/ /bag yod 'chi bar mi 'gyur te/ /bag med pa ni rtag
7a1(mdo 'grel): tu 'chi/ /de yi khyad par de rigs pas/ /mkhas pa rnams ni bag dang ldan/ /bag yod pa la rab dga' ba/ /'phags pa'i spyod yul dga' ba yin/ /de la rgyun tu bsgoms pa dang/ /rtag tu pha rol gnon brtan pa'i/ /brtan
7a2(mdo 'grel): pas grub bde bla med pa/ /mya ngan 'das la reg pa yin/ /gang tshe mkhas pas bag yod pas/ /bag med bcom pa de yi tshe/ /shes rab khang bzangs steng 'dzegs nas/ /mya ngan med pas gdungs bcas dang/ /brtan rnams ri
7a3(mdo 'grel): bo'i spo dag las/ /sa stengs byis pa rnams la blta/ /brtson 'grus dang ni bag yod dang/ /yang dag sdom dang dul ba yis/ /mkhas pas gling du byas nas ni/ /chu bo chen po mngon du zlog /brtson 'grus ldan zhing dran dang ldan
7a4(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ /spyod pa gtsang zhing brtags nas byed pa dang/ /yang dag sdom dang chos kyis 'tsho ba dang/ /bag yod rnams kyis grags pa mngon par 'phel/ /lhag pa'i sems la bag bya ste/ /thub pa'i thub gzhi rnams la bslab/ /
7a5(mdo 'grel): nyer zhi rtag tu dran ldan pa'i/ /skyob pa mya ngan med pa yin/ /dman pa'i chos la mi brten cing/ /bag med pa la brten mi bya/ /log par lta la 'dod med dang/ /'jig rten 'phel bar mi bya'o/ /'jig rten pa yi yang dag lta/ /chen
7a6(mdo 'grel): po su la yod gyur pa/ /de ni tshe rabs stong du yang/ /ngan 'gror 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro/ /bag med pa la spyod byed pa/ /skye bo byis pa bsam brlag yin/ /tshong dpon nor rnams srung ba ltar/ /mkhas pas bag dang ldan par bya/ /bag med
7a7(mdo 'grel): pa la mi sbyor zhing/ /'dod la dga' ba mi sogs dang/ /rtag tu bag yod sems byed pa/ /zag ba zad pa thob par 'gyur/ /zag pa zad pa ma thob kyang/ /dus 'dir bag med mi bya ste/ /ri dags ma yis seng ge ltar/ /bag med pa dag
7b1(mdo 'grel): gsad par 'gyur/ /bag med pha rol bud med bsten byed pa'i/ /mi gang yin la gnas skabs 'di bzhi 'byung/ /bsod nams mi thob bde bar mi nyal dang/ /gsum pa smad 'gyur bzhi pa dmyal bar 'gyur/ /bsod nams ma thob sdig pa'i
7b2(mdo 'grel): 'gro ba dang/ /'jigs dang bag tsha lhan cig bde ba chung/ /rgyal po'i chad pa chen pos gcod 'gyur zhing/ /lus zhig sems can dmyal ba rnams su 'tshed/ /gang zhig bdag bde lta 'dod pa/ /des ni gong ma bzhin du bya/ /byis pa'i shing
7b3(mdo 'grel): rta bzhin 'gyur bas/ /brtan pas brtson 'grus zhan mi bya/ /dper na byis pa'i shing rta dag /lam chen bzang po bor nas su/ /lam ngan dag tu 'gro byed pas/ /mig chag sems khongs chud pa ltar/ /de bzhin chos ni spangs nas kyang//
7b4(mdo 'grel): chos min rjes su 'jug byed pa'i/ /byis pa 'chi bdag dbang 'gro zhing/ /mig chag bzhin du bcom pa 'thob/ /gang zhig bya ba rnam spangs nas/ /mi bya ba dag byed pa dang/ /bag med pa yis rlom byed pa/ /de dag rnams kyis zag pa 'phel//
7b5(mdo 'grel): gang gi zag pa 'phel 'gyur ba/ /de yi zag med rgyang ma na/ /gang zhig lus rtogs dran pa dang/ /rtag tu legs par brtsams pa dang/ /bya ba ma yin mi byed cing/ /rgyun tu bya ba byed pa dang/ /dran dang shes bzhin ldan pa de'i/ /zag pa rnams
7b6(mdo 'grel): ni zad par 'gyur/ /gang gi zag pa zad gyur pa/ /de ni zag med thob par 'gyur/ /ji tsam mang du smra byed pa/ /de dag dam chos 'dzin ma yin/ /gang dag 'di na thos nyung yang/ /lus kyis chos dag mngon sum byas/ /gang dag chos la bag
7b7(mdo 'grel): byed pa/ /de dag dam chos 'dzin pa yin/ /gal te rigs bcas mang du smras kyang ni/ /bag med mi dag de ltar byed mi 'gyur/ /dper na phyugs rdzi gzhan gyi phyugs bgrangs ltar/ /de dag dge sbyong skal ba thob ma yin/ /gal te rigs can nyung
8a1(mdo 'grel): ngu smra byed kyang/ /chos kyi rjes su chos la spyod pa dang/ /'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug spong byed pa/ /de dag dge sbyong skal pa thob pa yin/ /bag yod bsngags pa brjod byed cing/ /rtag tu bag med la smos pas/ /bag yod
8a2(mdo 'grel): mchod sbyin brgya pa yang/ /lha rnams nang na gtso bor 'gyur/ /bya ba byas rung ma byas rung/ /mkhas pa bag yod bsngags pa brjod/ /bag dang bcas pa'i mkhas pa yis/ /don gnyis rab tu len par byed/ /tshe 'di'i don ni gang yin
8a3(mdo 'grel): dang/ phyi ma'i don ni gang yin pa/ /de dag brtan pas rtogs pas na/ /mkhas pa zhes ni brjod pa yin/ /dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing/ /bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/ /bdag nyid ngan 'gro las 'dren te/ /'dam rdzab las ni
8a4(mdo 'grel): glang chen bzhin/ /dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing/ /bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/ /sdig pa'i chos rnams sprul par byed/ /rlung gis ljon shing lo ma bzhin/ /dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing/ /bag med pa la 'jigs lta
8a5(mdo 'grel): bas kun tu sbyor ba phra sbom dag /me yis bsregs pa bzhin du 'gro/ /dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing/ /bag med pa la 'jig lta bas/ /kun tu sbyor ba kun zad pa/ /rims kyis nyams su myong bar 'gyur/ /dge slong bag yod
8a6(mdo 'grel): la dga' zhing/ /bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/ /'du byed nyer zhi zhi ba yi/ /zhi ba'i go 'phang so sor rtogs/ /dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing/ /bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/ /mya ngan 'das dang nye ba'i phyir/ /yongs su nyams
8a7(mdo 'grel): 'gyur mi srid do/ /brtson 'grus ldan zhing bag yod dang/ /chos spyod legs par spyod byed la/ /'jig rten 'di dang pha rol du/ /chos spyad pas ni bde ba 'thob/ /zhi phyir bslab pa la brten dang/ /rtsol ba dang ni brtson 'grus bskyed/ /mi dran
8b1(mdo 'grel): pa dang bag med dang/ /brtson 'grus chung dang kun sdom med/ /gnyid dang snyoms dang g.yeng ba ste/ /'di dag bslab pa'i bar chad pas/ /khyed kyis yan lag der rtogs la/ /dran pa chud ni ma gsan cig /dge slong tshul khrims bzang ba dang/ /
8b2(mdo 'grel): bag yod pa la dga' ba yis/ /kun rtogs legs par mnyam zhog ste/ /rang gi sems ni rjes su bsrungs/ /brtsam par bya zhing 'byung bar bya/ /sangs rgyas bstan la 'jug par bya/ /dam+bu'i khyim la glang chen bzhin/ /'chi bdag sde ni
8b3(mdo 'grel): gzhom par bya/ /gang zhig chos 'dul 'di la ni/ /bag dang ldan par spyod byed pa/ /skye ba'i 'khor pa rab spangs nas/ /sdug bsngal tha mar byed par 'gyur/ /bag yod pa'i tshoms te bzhi pa'o// //sdug pa rnams las mya ngan skye/ /
8b4(mdo 'grel): sdug pa rnams las 'jigs pa skye/ /sdug pa dag ni rnams spangs na/ /mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa med/ /sdug gu ma las mya ngan skye/ /sdug las sdug bsngal sdug las 'jigs/ /sdug gu ma dag gzhan gyur na/ /yi mug 'byung
8b5(mdo 'grel): ba thob par byed/ /'jig rten sdug bsngal rnam pa du ma dang/ /mya ngan smre sngags 'don pa ji snyed pa/ /de dag sdug pa dag las brten te 'byung/ /sdug pa spangs na de dag yod mi 'gyur/ /gang phyir 'jig rten 'ga' na'ang sdug med pa/ /
8b6(mdo 'grel): gang yin de dag bde zhing mya ngan med/ /de bas gdung med rdul bral don gnyer bas/ /nam yang sdug par byed pa de mi bya/ /sdug pa ma mthong sdug bsngal la/ /mi sdug mthong na'ang de bzhin pas/ /nam yang sdug dang phrad mi bya/ /mi sdug dang
8b7(mdo 'grel): yang phrad mi bya/ /sdug pa dang ni bye bral dang/ /mi sdug pa dang phrad pa yis/ /gang gi mi dag dga' byed pa/ /mya ngan mi bzad skye bar 'gyur/ /sdug pa shi bar gyur pa na/ /gnyen 'dun mdza' bshes mang po dag /yun ring dus su mya ngan dang/ /
9a1(mdo 'grel): sdug dang bral bas sdug bsngal 'gyur/ /gang la sdug dang sdug min med/ /de la mdud pa yod min pas/ /de ltas sdug nyid sdig can la/ /sdug par byed par mi bya'o/ /sdug la bltas te don btab nas/ /bde sbyor rnams la
9a2(mdo 'grel): mi 'jug cing/ /bdag nyid mi bde'i sbyor ldan dang/ /bde sbyor don ldan rnams la smon/ /gzugs sdug bde bas bsdams pa dag /lha mi so so'i ris dag tu/ /sdig pa byed cing yongs nyams nas/ /rga dang 'chi ba'i dbang du 'gro /gang zhig
9a3(mdo 'grel): nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /bag yod gzugs sdug spong byed pa/ /des ni spang dka' bdud zas dang/ /sdig pa'i rtsa ba'ang drungs nas phyung/ /legs min legs pa'i tshul dang ni/ /sdug min sdug pa'i tshul gyis dang/ /sdug bsngal bde ba'i tshul gyis su//
9a4(mdo 'grel): bag med rnams ni mngon du 'joms/ /gal te bdag la dga' byed na/ /nyes par byed pas bde ba dag /bde blag kho nar mi 'thob pas/ /'di ni sdig la gzhug mi bya/ /gal te bdag la dga' byed na/ /legs par byed pas bde ba dag /bde blag kho
9a5(mdo 'grel): nar thob 'gyur bar/ /'di ni sdig la gzhug mi bya/ /dper na dgon pa'i grong khyer dag /brtan pa'i 'obs kyis bskor ba ltar/ /gal te bdag la dga' byed na/ /'di ni bsrung bas legs par bsrung/ /gal te bdag la dga' byed na/ /thun gsum
9a6(mdo 'grel): gang yang rung ba la/ /mkhas pas mel tshe bya ba yis/ /'di ni sba bas legs par sba/ /dper na dgon pa'i grong khyer dag /phyi nang srung bar byed pa ltar/ /dal 'byor chud ni mi zos pa/ /de ltar bdag ni bsrung bar bya/ /sems can dmyal bar skye
9a7(mdo 'grel): na yang/ /dal 'byor thal bas 'gyod par 'ong/ /phyogs rnams kun tu sems kyis yongs brtags kyang/ /bdag las ches sdug 'ga' yang ma mthong bas/ /de ltar so sor gzhan la'ang rang sdug pas/ /de phyir bdag gis gzhan la gnod mi bya/
9b1(mdo 'grel): thams cad la'ang srog ni sdug /thams cad chad pas 'jigs pas na/ /ngang gi nyams la dpag gyis te/ /brdeg par mi bya gsang mi bya/ /rgyangs thag chad par sbyugs pa'i mi/ /ring nas nyes zho med 'ongs na/ /gnyen bshes mdza' bo lhags nas su/ /a
9b2(mdo 'grel): la la zhes mngon par dga' / /de bzhin bsod nams byas pa'i mi/ /'jig rten 'di nas pha rol du/ /phyin tshe gnyen bzhin bsod nams dag /'ongs nas mngon par dga' bar byed/ /de bas 'jig rten pha rol gyi/ /ched du bsod nams bsags
9b3(mdo 'grel): par gyis/ /bsod nams 'jig rten pha rol tu/ /lus can rnams kyi gnas su 'gyur/ /gang zhig legs par spyad spyod pa'i/ /dge ba lha rnams bstod par byed/ /'di na 'ang smad par mi 'gyur la/ /mtho ris su yang dga' ba 'thob/ /chos gnas
9b4(mdo 'grel): tshul khrims phun sum tshogs/ /ngo tsha shes shing bden par smra/ /rang gi bya ba byed pa la/ /skye bo gzhan rnams dga' bar byed/ /rang gi don ni byed pa la/ /'di ltar gzhan rnams dga' 'gyur zhing/ /mthong ba'i chos la bsngags pa dang/ /pha rol
9b5(mdo 'grel): tu yang bde 'gror 'gyur/ /gtams na na pa'i tshig smra dang/ /mi rigs spyod las bzlog pa las/ /dam pa rnams ni dga' bar byed/ /dam pa ma yin dga' mi 'gyur/ /de bas mchog dang mchog min pa/ /shi 'phos bral bar gyur pa na/ /dam
9b6(mdo 'grel): pa ma yin dmyal bar 'gro/ /dam pa mtho ris 'gro bar 'gyur/ /sdug pa'i tshoms te lnga pa'o// //bsngags par 'gyur dang nor 'thob dang/ /pha rol bde 'gro dga' 'gyur ba'i/ /bde ba gsum po don gnyer ba'i/ /mkhas pas tshul
9b7(mdo 'grel): khrims bsrung bar bya/ /'phags dang mthong ba phun tshogs dang/ /'jig rten zhi ba rten 'gyur ba'i/ /gnas gzhan 'di dag mthong ba yi/ /mkhas pas tshul khrims bsrung bar bya/ /lus la yongs su gdung med par/ /tshul khrims kyis ni bde ba
10a1(mdo 'grel): 'thob/ /mtshan mo bde bar nyal ba dang/ /sad pa na'ang dga' bar 'gyur/ /sbyin dang tshul khrims ldan pa dag /mkhas pas byin pa'i bsod nams kyis/ /'di dag pha rol dag tu yang/ /rtag tu bde ba thob par 'gyur/ /rgan pa'i bar
10a2(mdo 'grel): la tshul khrims so dge /dad pa rab tu gnas na legs/ /mi yi rin chen shes rab ste/ /bsod nams tshom pos dbrog ba dka' / /dge slong tshul khrims la gnas shing/ /dbang po rnams dang bsdams pa dang/ /zas kyi ched ni rig pa dang/ /
10a3(mdo 'grel): mi nyal ba la 'bad pa ste/ /de ltar gnas par brtson pa dang/ /nyin mtshan snyom las mi byed pa/ /mya ngan 'das dang nyi ba'i phyir/ /yongs su nyams 'gyur mi srid do/ /mi ni tshul khrims la gnas nas/ /sems dang shes rab bsgom pa la//
10a4(mdo 'grel): brtson zhing nges gnas dge slong gis/ /sdug bsngal zad pa thob par 'gyur/ /de phyir rtag tu tshul khrims dang/ /ting 'dzin tshul khrims bsrung ba dang/ /lhag mthong la ni bslab pa dang/ /shes bzhin so sor dran par bya/ /des ni kun sbyor
10a5(mdo 'grel): zang byas nas/ /yid 'bral lhag ma med 'gyur te/ /lus zhig shes rab ldan pa yis/ /bgrang du med pa'i mya ngan 'das/ /gang zhig tshul khrims ting 'dzin dang/ /shes rab 'di gsum legs bsgoms te/ /shin tu dri med mthar phyin cing/
10a6(mdo 'grel): gdung med yang srid zad 'gyur dang/ /chags pa'i 'ching las rnam grol zhing/ /lus spangs shes rab ldan pa dang/ /bdud kyi yul las 'das pa dag /nyi ma bzhin du lam med 'bad/ dge slong phyi dang nang nyid la/ /bag med rlom par byed pa
10a7(mdo 'grel): yi/ tshul khrims ting 'dzin shes rab rnams/ /yongs su rdzogs par mi 'gyur ro/ /sprin gyis khebs las char 'bab cing/ /nam thang ba las char mi 'bab/ /de bas khebs pa sol cig dang/ /'di ltar char pa 'bab mi 'gyur/ /de ltar
10b1(mdo 'grel): rtag tu mthong ba dang/ dge slong tshul khrims sdom pa yin/ /mya ngan 'das par 'gro ba'i lam/ /myur ba kho nar rnam par dag /me tog dri ni rdzi phyogs yin mi 'gro/ /rtsa ba rgyas spos tsan dan rnams kyang min/ /dam pa'i dri ni rdzi phyogs min 'gro ste/ /
10b2(mdo 'grel): phyogs rnams kun tu mi mchog dri yis khyab/ /rgya spos dang ni tsan dan dang/ /utpa la dang ma li ka/ /spos kyi rigs ni 'di dag pas/ /tshul khrims dri bsung phul du phyin/ /rgya spos tsan dan gang yin pa'i/ /dri bsung 'di ni chung ngu na/ /tshul
10b3(mdo 'grel): khrims ldan pa'i dri bsung kang/ /des ni bde dang mtho ris khyab/ /de ltar bag yod gnas bya zhing/ /tshul khrims rnam par dag par bya/ /yang dag shes pas rnam grol na/ /bdud kyi lam ni rnyed mi 'gyur/ /'di ni bde bar 'gro lam ste/ /rnam par
10b4(mdo 'grel): dag byed lam 'di la/ rab tu bsgrims te bsgoms nas kyang/ /bdud kyi 'ching ba spang par gyis/ /tshul khrims kyi tshoms drug pa'o// //lus kyi nyes par spyod spang zhing/ /lus kyi legs spyad spyad pa'i phyir/ /lus kyi nyes
10b5(mdo 'grel): chen las gsungs na/ /lus ni bsdams pa byas par 'gyur/ /ngag gi nyes par spyod spang zhing/ /ngag gi legs spyad spyad pa'i phyir/ /ngag gi nyes chen las bsrungs na/ /ngag ni bsdams pa byas par 'gyur/ /yid kyi nyes par spyod spang zhing/ /
10b6(mdo 'grel): yid kyi legs spyad spyad pa'i phyir/ /yid kyi nyes chen las bsrungs na/ /yid ni bsdams pa byas par 'gyur/ /lus kyi nyes par spyod spang zhing/ /ngag gi nyes par spyod pa spang/ /yid kyi nyes par spyod spang zhing/ /spyon gzhan ldan pa gang
10b7(mdo 'grel): yin spang/ /lus kyi dge ba rnams bya zhing/ /ngag gi dge ba phal cher bya/ /yid kyi dge ba rnams bya zhing/ /tshad med bzhi dang bral mi bya/ /lus kyi dge ba rnams bya zhing/ /ngag dang yid kyis byas na ni/ /'di dang pha rol dag tu yang/ /rtag tu bde
11a1(mdo 'grel): ba thob par 'gyur/ /rtag tu lus ni bsdams pa'i phyir/ /thub pa 'tshe ba med pa yin/ /de ni 'chi med gnas 'gro zhing/ /gang du song na 'ang mya ngan med/ /rtag tu dag ni bsdams pa'i phyir/ /thub pa 'tshe ba med pa yin/ /de ni
11a2(mdo 'grel): 'chi med gnas 'gro zhing/ /gang du song na'ang mya ngan med/ /rtag tu yid ni bsdams pa'i phyir/ /thub pa 'tshe ba med pa yin/ /de ni 'chi med gnas 'gro zhing/ /gang du song na'ang mya ngan med/ /brtan pa rnams kyis lus bsdams shing/ /
11a3(mdo 'grel): brten pa rnams kyis dag kyang bsdams/ /brtan pa rnams kyis yid bsdams shing/ /brtan pas kun tu bsdams byas ni/ /de dag 'chi med gnas 'gro zhing/ /gang du song na'ang mya ngan med/ /lus kyi sdom pa legs pa ste/ /ngag gi sdom
11a4(mdo 'grel): pa legs pa yin/ /yid kyi sdom pa'ang legs pa ste/ /thams cad du ni sdom pa legs/ /kun tu bsdams pa'i dge slong ni/ /sdug bsngal kun las rab tu grol/ /ngag rnams bsrung zhing yid rnams legs bsdams te/ /lus kyi mi dge
11a5(mdo 'grel): ba dag spyad mi bya/ /las lam gsum po 'di dag rnam sbyangs na/ /drang srong gsungs pa'i lam ni thob par 'gyur/ /legs par spyad pa'i tshoms te bdun pa'o// //gang dag byas bzhin ma byas zer ba dang/ /rdzun du smra ba dmyal
11a6(mdo 'grel): bar 'gro bar 'gyur/ /mi de gnyi ga 'dra ba pha rol tu/ /song nas dman pa'i chos dang ldan par 'gyur/ /skyes bu skyes pa'i kha nas ni/ /tshig ngan smra bar byed pa yi/ /tshig gi sta re skyes gyur nas/ /bdag nyid gcod par byed par 'gyur//
11a7(mdo 'grel): gang zhig smad 'os skye bo bstod byed dang/ /bstod 'os skye bo rnam par smod byed pa/ /de ni kha yi 'thab krol kun sogs shing/ /'thab krol can gang nges ni bde mi thob/ /gang 'dir tshe los rang nor pham byed pa/ /'thab krol de ni chung zad
11b1(mdo 'grel): tsam du zad/ /gang zhig bde bar gshegs la yid 'khrugs pa/ /de 'dir 'thab kol shin tu chen po yin/ /ngag yid 'phags pas smad pa'i 'jig rten na/ /bye bar chu bur can dang stong phag ni/ /bzhi bcu gcig tu chu bur rdol ba yi/ /
11b2(mdo 'grel): sems can dmyal ba rnams su 'gro bar 'gyur/ /sdig pa'i sems kyis ma nyes skyon brjod pa/ /bdag nyid gsad phyir dmyal ba spel bar zad/ /stobs ldan nyes med pa dag bzod byed cing/ /de la sems kyang 'khrugs par mi byed do/ /bsam
11b3(mdo 'grel): brlag gang zhig sdig can gyi/ /lta la brten nas 'phags pa na/ /dgra bcom chos kyis 'tsho ba dang/ /bstan pa spong bar byed pa dag /smig ma 'bru chags lta bu ni/ /de ni rang gi 'bras bu gsod/ /tshig bzang kho na smra bya yi/ /sdig pa can
11b4(mdo 'grel): dag smra mi bya/ /sdig can gdung byed smra ba bas/ /tshig bzang smra bar byed pa rung/ /byis pa sdig can smra byed pa/ /smra ba'i tshe na 'chid 'gyur la/ /gal te smras na gzhan stong pa/ /de dag 'phags pa mi gsung ngo/ /
11b5(mdo 'grel): dge slong dag ni bsdams pa dang/ /dal bus smra zhing rlom pa med/ /gang zhig chos ldan don ston pa/ /de ni snyan par smra ba yin/ /legs par smra ba mchog ces 'phags pa gsung/ /snyan smra mi snyan ma yin de
11b6(mdo 'grel): gnyis pa/ /bden smra brdzun pa ma yin de gsum pa/ /chos smra phal pa ma yin bzhi pa de'o/ /tshig de rnams ni smra bya zhing/ /gang gis bdag kyang mi gdung la/ /pha rol la yang gnod med pa'i/ /tshig de legs par
11b7(mdo 'grel): smra bar bya/ /gang gis mngon par dga' 'gyur zhing/ /gang gis sdig pa mi bskyed dang/ /smras pas pha rol dga' 'gyur ba'i/ /snyan tshig kha nas smra bar bya/ /bden pa'i tshig ni bdud rtsi ste/ /bden pa'i tshig
12a1(mdo 'grel): ni bla med yin/ /don dang chos la rab gnas pa/ /bden pa yin zhes dam pa gsung/ /sdug bsngal thams cad spang ba'i phyir/ /sangs rgyas kyi ni gsungs tshig gang/ /bden pa mya ngan 'das 'gro ba'i/ /tshig
12a2(mdo 'grel): de bla na med pa yin/ /tshig gi tshoms te brgyad pa'o// //chos gcig las ni rab 'das shing/ /'jig rten pha rol spyo ba yi/ /lus can brdzun du smra ba yi/ /sdig pa mi bya ci yang med/ /lcags sgong me lce
12a3(mdo 'grel): 'bar 'dra ba/ /thos par 'gyur ba ches sla yi/ /tshul 'chal legs par mi sdom pas/ /yul 'khor bsod snyoms bzar mi rung/ /khyod ni sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs shing/ /khyod la sdug bsngal mi sdug na/ /mngon
12a4(mdo 'grel): sum dag gam lkog tu 'ang rung/ /sdig pa can gyi las mi bya/ /gal te sdig pa'i las byas sam/ /byed kyang rung ste khyod kyis ni/ /kog ces langs te bros byas kyang/ /sdug bsngal las ni thar mi 'gyur/ /gang du gnas na
12a5(mdo 'grel): las kyis mi tshugs pa'i/ /sa phyogs de ni yod pa ma yin te/ /bar snang la med rgya mtsho'i nang na med/ /ri bo rnams kyi gseb tu zhugs kyang min/ /pha rol po la brtags nas gang/ /sdig pa can gyi las mthong ba/ /de
12a6(mdo 'grel): dag bdag gis mi bya ste/ /sdig byas las ni rjes su 'brang/ /las gang shin tu mi bzang dang/ /zol byed gzhal lugs 'chos pa dang/ /mi la 'tshe bar byed pa dang/ /gzhan la byed du 'jug pa yi/ /las de mi yi rjes 'breng bas
12a7(mdo 'grel): de yis g.yang sar ltung bar byed/ /mi yis dge ba'am sdig pa yi/ /las ni gang dang gang byas pa'i/ /las rnams chud zar mi 'gyur te/ /de lta de ltar 'bras bur 'gyur/ /de yi tshogs pa ji srid par/ /de srid 'di na gdung
12b1(mdo 'grel): bar byed/ /de la gzhan dag gdung byed de/ /gdung byed de ni brtags par 'gyur/ /'di ni bdag rjes mi 'phreng zhes/ /byis pa ma brtags byas pa yi/ /sdig pa'i las kyis 'gro ba dag /pha rol du ni shes par 'gyur/ /gal te byis pa mi
12b2(mdo 'grel): shes par/ /sdig pa'i las ni byas pa dag /nam zhig na ni de nyid kyis/ /rnam smin tsha ba so sor bsten/ /rang gi las kyis de 'og tu/ /me yis bsregs pa bzhin du gdungs/ /byis pa shes rab chung ngu dag /bdag la dgra bzhin byed
12b3(mdo 'grel): pa yis/ /gang zhig 'bras bu tshar 'gyur ba'i/ /sdig can las ni spyod par byed/ /gang zhig byas pas gdung 'gyur zhing/ /mchi mas gdong g.yogs du bzhin du/ /rnam smin so sor bsten pa yi/ /las de dag ni ma byas legs/ /
12b4(mdo 'grel): gang zhig byas na mi gdung zhing/ /dga' zhing yid ni bde ba yis/ /rnam smin so sor bsten pa yi/ /las de dag ni byas na legs/ /bdag nyid bde ba 'dod pa'i phyir/ /dgod bzhin sdig pa'i las byas pa'i/ /sdig las de yi rnam smin dag
12b5(mdo 'grel): du bzhin nyams su myong bar 'gyur/ /nges par sdig las 'phral du ni/ /'o ma lta bur 'gyur mi byed/ /thal bas g.yogs pa'i me lta bur/ /nges ni byis pa sreg par byed/ /sdig las 'phral du nges par ni/ /mtshon bzhin gcod par mi
12b6(mdo 'grel): byed kyang/ /sdig pa'i las kyis 'gro ba dag /pha rol tu ni mngon par 'gyur/ /gang du de dag rnam smin ni/ /tsha ba so sor brten pa yi/ /sdig pa'i las kyi 'gro ba dag /pha rol tu ni shes par 'gyur/ /lcags las g.ya' ni langs
12b7(mdo 'grel): gyur pa/ /langs pa des ni de nyid za/ /de bzhin ma brtags byas pa yi/ /rang gi las kyis ngan 'gror 'gro /las kyi choms te dgu pa'o// //ngang dang tshul khrims sbyin pa ste/ /chos 'di rnams ni skyes bu dam pas bsngags
13a1(mdo 'grel): 'di yis lha'i 'jig rten 'gro 'gyur zhing/ /lam 'di nyid kyis lha yul 'gro zhes gsungs/ /'jungs rnams lha yi 'jig rten mi 'gro zhing/ /de yis byis pa sbyin pa'i bsngags mi brjod/ /brtan rnams byin la rjes su yi
13a2(mdo 'grel): rang ba/ /des ni de dag gzhan du bde ba myong/ /'di ni skyes bu nor mchog dad pa ste/ /'di na chos la legs spyod bde ba 'thob/ /bde ba kho na ro bro rnams kyi phul/ /shes rab kyis 'tsho 'tsho ba'i mchog ces gsungs/ /mya ngan 'das par
13a3(mdo 'grel): 'gro ba yi/ /dgra bcom chos la dad bskyed de/ /mkhas pas gus par mnyan na ni/ /de dang de ye shes rab 'thob/ /bag can gyis ni rgya mtsho dang/ /dad pas chu bo rnams las grol/ /brtson 'grus kyis ni sdug bsngal spong/ /shes rab
13a4(mdo 'grel): kyis ni yongs dag 'gyur/ /dge slong dad pa'i grogs ldan zhing/ /shes rab kyis ni gtams pa dang/ /mya ngan 'das par mngon dga' bas/ /'ching ba thams cad gcod par 'gyur/ /gang gis dad dang tshul khrims dang/ /shes
13a5(mdo 'grel): rab nyid ni legs bsgoms shing/ /mkhas pas skyon rnams spong ba de/ /legs pa'i ngang tshul can zhes brjod/ /dad dang tshul khrims phun sum tshogs/ /gtong ldan 'jungs pa rnams spangs pa/ /de ni gang dang gar sor ba/ /de dang
13a6(mdo 'grel): der ni mchod par 'gyur/ /mkhas gang 'tsho ba'i 'jig rten na/ /dad dang shes rab sten byed pa/ /de dag de yi nor mchog ste/ /de yi nor gzhan phal bar zad/ /'phags pa lta bar 'dod pa dang/ /dam chos nyan par
13a7(mdo 'grel): dga' ba dang/ /ser sna'i dri ma rnams spangs pa/ /de ni dad pa can zhes bya/ /dad pa'i lam rgyags bkur bar bya/ /bsod nams chom pos dpog mi nus/ /chom rkun 'phrog par byed pa zlog /dge slong rnams kyis blangs na dga' //
13b1(mdo 'grel): mkhas pas dge sbyong 'ongs pa la/ /mngon par dga' bar byed 'gyur zhing/ /skye bo rnams ni ci rigs par/ /dad pa ji bzhin sbyin byed cing/ /gzhan gyi zas dang skom de la/ /gang zhig yid ni mi bde ba/ /des ni nyin dang
13b2(mdo 'grel): mtshan rnams su/ /ting 'dzin thob par mi 'gyur ro/ /gang gis ta la mgo bcad ltar/ /de 'dra kun tu gcod byed pa/ /des ni nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /ting nge 'dzin dag thob par 'gyur/ /khron pa skam po ji lta bas/ /dad
13b3(mdo 'grel): pa med pa bsten mi bya/ /ji ste de la yongs bskos kyang/ /'dam chu dring 'byung bar zad/ /chu mang rnam par dad pa dang/ /bsil bar gyur cing rlog med pa'i/ /mtsho la chu 'dod ji lta bar/ /shes rab can gyis dang ldan bsten//
13b4(mdo 'grel): chags sam ma chags kyang rung ste/ /de yis thub sku mi spang bas/ /ma dad pa dag spang bar bya/ /dad pa rnams ni nye bar bsten/ /dad pa'i tshoms te bcu pa'o// //sdom la mi rtag 'dod dang srang ba dang/ /bag yod de bzhin
13b5(mdo 'grel): dga' ba dang/ /tshul khrims legs spyod tshig dag dang/ /las dang dad pa de dag bcu/ /bram zes 'dod par ba spang zhing/ /brtson 'grus kyis ni rgyun chod cig /'dod pa rab tu ma spangs par/ /thub pa gcig gis mi thob po//
13b6(mdo 'grel): kun tu rgyu ba zhan pa dag /nyon mongs phyir yang kun sogs pas/ /brtson 'grus brtan pa kho na yis/ /bya ba de nyid byed la rag /gzhan pa'i lam ni ji snyed pa/ /kun nas nyon mongs dka' thub dang/ /tshangs spyod yongs su
13b7(mdo 'grel): ma dag de/ /don chen 'gyur snyam mi byed do/ /ji ltar mnga' ni gzung nyes pas/ /lag pa tshod par gyur pa ltar/ /dge sbyong bsrung ba bya nyes pas/ /dmyal bar nye bar khrid par byed/ /ji ltar mda' ni gzung legs pas//
14a1(mdo 'grel): lag pa chod par mi 'gyur ltar/ /dge sbyong bsrung ba bya legs na/ /mya ngan 'das par nye bar 'dren/ /dge sbyong rnam par ma shes dang/ /brgal bar dka' dang bzod dga' dang/ /gang dag zhen pa 'gyod pa yi/ /sdug
14a2(mdo 'grel): bsngal mang po de dag 'byung/ /yang dang yang du 'gyod pa yi/ /kun rtog dbang du 'gro ba yi/ /sems ni bzlog par ma byas par/ /dge sbyong spyod pa ma byas pas/ /nyes par rab byung nyes dga' ba/ /khyim 'dug nyes rtsom byed pa
14a3(mdo 'grel): dag /sdug bsngal mnyam med bsten pa dag /yang srid sdug bsngal sogs par zad/ /tshem bu ngur smrig gon pa dag /phal cher yang dag mi sdom cing/ /sdig pa'i chos can sdig la dga' / /sdig can de dag ngan 'gror 'gro//
14a4(mdo 'grel): sa la'i shing la 'khril shing ltar/ /gang zhig shin tu khrims 'chal te/ /ji ltar rang la dgra bzhin du/ /de ni de ltar byed par 'dod/ /mgo bo skye bor gyur bar dra/ /da dung rgan rabs ma chud pa/ /de ni lang cho gtugs pa ste/ /de ni
14a5(mdo 'grel): rgun bran zhes bya'o/ /gang zhig dge dang sdig pa dag /spangs shing tshangs par spyod pa dang/ /sde tshogs spangs nas spyod byed pa/ /de ni rgan rabs zhes bya'o/ /brtul zhugs med cing rdzun smra na/ /mgo bo bregs tsam dge sbyong min/
14a6(mdo 'grel): rmongs pa 'dod la zhugs pa dag /ji ga dge sbyong yin nam kye/ /brtul zhugs med cing brdzun smra na/ /mgo bo brags tsam dge sbyong min/ /gang zhig sdig pa zhi gyur de/ /mkhas pas dge sbyong yin par shes/ /brtul
14a7(mdo 'grel): zhugs med cing brdzun smra na/ /mgo bo bregs tsam dge sbyong min/ /gang dag sdig pa che phra dag /kun la brtags nas byed pa dang/ /sdig pa zhi ba de dag ni/ /dge sbyong nyid ces brjod par bya/ /sdig pa spangs pa bram ze ste//
14b1(mdo 'grel): zhi bar spyod pa dge sbyong yin/ /bdag gi dri ma rab spangs pa/ /des na rab tu byung zhes brjod/ /dge sbyong gi tshoms te bcu gcig pa'o// //gang tshe 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi/ /shes rab kyis ni mthong ba dang/ /lam 'dir
14b2(mdo 'grel): rab tu shes pa yis/ /srid pa'i sred pa rab tu 'dral/ /dper na rlung gis rdul bslang ba/ /char pa bab pas zhi byed ltar/ /gang tshe shes rab kyis mthong ba/ /de tshe kun rtog zhi bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig legs par rtog pa yi/ /skye shi
14b3(mdo 'grel): legs par zad 'gyur zhing/ /'jig rten nges 'byed 'gyur ba yi/ /shes rab de ni gtso bo yin/ /bden pa'i nang na bden bzhi dang/ /lam nang yang dag brgyad pa mchog /rkang gnyis nang na mig can dang/ /chos kyi nang na chags
14b4(mdo 'grel): bral mchog /'du byed thams cad mi rtag par/ /gang tshe shes rab kyis mthong ba/ /de tshe sdug bsngal las yid 'byung/ /lam 'di rnam par dag par 'gyur/ /'du byed thams cad sdug bsngal bar/ /gang tshe shes rab kyis mthong
14b5(mdo 'grel): ba/ /gang tshe sdug bsngal las yid 'byung/ /lam 'di rnam par dag par 'gyur/ /'du byed thams cad stong nyid du/ /gang tshe shes rab kyis mthong ba/ /de tshe sdug bsngal las yid 'byung/ /lam 'di rnam par dag par 'gyur//
14b6(mdo 'grel): 'du byed thams cad bdag med par/ /gang tshe shes rab kyis mthong ba/ /de tshe sdug bsngal las yid 'byung/ /lo ma 'di rnam par dag par 'gyur/ /sred pa'i zug rngu gcod byed lam/ /ngas ni khyed cag rnams la bstan/ /
14b7(mdo 'grel): de bzhin gshegs pa ston pa ste/ /khyed cag rnams kyis bya dgos so/ /srid pa'i zug rngu sel ba'i lam/ /ngas ni khyed cag rnams la bstan/ /de bzhin gshegs pa ston pa ste/ /khyed cag rnams kyis bya dgos so/ /lta ba rnam
15a1(mdo 'grel): par dag byed dang/ /lam 'di ma gtogs gzhan mod pas/ /ting nge 'dzin la rab zhugs te/ /bdud kyi 'ching ba spang bar gyis/ /'di ni drang lam pha rol gnon pa ste/ /mtsho la dad pa'i srang ltar bgrod bya ba
15a2(mdo 'grel): shAkya thub pas mnyam bzhag gang rtogs nas/ /tshogs la yang dang yang du bshad pa 'di/ /skye shi'i mdza' rtogs phan mdzad thugs brtse bas/ /bgrod pa gcig lam rab tu bstan mdzad pa'i/ /lam 'di chu bo rnams
15a3(mdo 'grel): las mngon brgal zhing/ /de bzhin rgal bar 'gyur zhing brgal bar mdzad/ /shin tu mthar gtugs gdul bya dag bya dang/ /mkhor ba'i skye shi zad par bya ba dang/ /khams rnams du ma so sor rtogs bya'i phyir/ /spyan dang
15a4(mdo 'grel): ldan bas lam 'di rab tu bstan/ /ji ltar chu klung gang+gA'i chu rgyun shugs/ /rgya mtsho'i nang du 'bab par 'gyur ba ltar/ /de bzhin shes rab yangs pas bstan pa'i lam/ /'di ni 'chi med shes rab thob phyir
15a5(mdo 'grel): 'jug /gang zhig 'byung po kun la thugs brtse bas/ /sngon chad ma thos chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ /skyob pa lha dang mi rnams 'dul mdzad pa/ /srid pa'i mthar phyin de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnam rtog dge ba gsum
15a6(mdo 'grel): ni bstan bya zhing/ /dge ba ma yin gsum yang rnam par spang/ /kun nas rdul las char gyis mnan pa ltar/ /de nas rtag dang dpyod pa zhi bar bya/ /de nas sems la rnam rtog nyer zhi na/ /bla med byang chub bde la reg par
15a7(mdo 'grel): 'gyur/ /ting 'dzin gsum po rnams la yid gtang cing/ /dben pa las skyes tshang med bsgom par bya/ /dran ldan mkhas pas mdung pa zhi bya zhing/ /gsum po rnams kyis rnam gsum rab tu dral/ /shes rab mtshon
15b1(mdo 'grel): dang brtson 'grus stobs dang ldan/ /dran ldan mnyam gzhag ting 'dzin la dga' bas/ /'jig rten skye dang 'jig par rtogs nas ni/ /kun nas rab tu rnam grol de rig yin/ /'jig rten tha ma legs par rtogs gyur nas/ /'jig
15b2(mdo 'grel): rten mthar son pha rol phyin ces brjod/ /gang zhig zhi ba 'phags lam yan lag brgyad/ /lam drang bsgoms pa des ni bdud rtsi rnyed/ /de ltar spyod pas bde 'dod bde ba 'thob/ /snyan pa thob cing grags pa 'phel bar 'byung
15b3(mdo 'grel): lam gyi tshoms te bcu gnyis pa'o// /ched du brjod pa'i tshoms bam pa gnyis pa/ /dre'u mo rang gi mngal gyis dang/ /'dam bu smig ma 'bras bus dang/ /chu shing 'bras bus phung ba ltar/ /pho shal bkur bstis
15b4(mdo 'grel): phung bar 'gyur/ /ji srid blun po mchod byas pa/ /de srid rab tu brlag par 'gyur/ /byis pa dkar po'i cha 'grib cing/ /de yi spyi bo'ang nges par nyams/ /ngan pa rnyed pa 'dod pa dang/ /dge slong 'khor ni 'dod pa dang/ /gnas
15b5(mdo 'grel): la ser sna byed pa dag /rigs gzhan dag gis mtshong ba dang/ /rab tu byung dang khyim pa dag /gang yang rung ba bdag 'phrigs te/ /bya ba byas rung ma byas rung/ /bdag dbang gyur na re stes zhes/ /de ltar byis pa kun rtog na/ /sems
15b6(mdo 'grel): la 'dod chen 'phel bar 'gyur/ /rnyed pa'i thabs ni gzhan yin la/ /mya ngan 'das 'gro gzhan yin zhes/ /de ltar ci rigs shes nas su/ /bkur sti dag la mi dga' zhing/ /dben pa rim gyis 'phel byed pa'i/ /dge slong
15b7(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas nyan thos yin/ /thams cad la ni mi rtsal zhing/ /mi yis 'phrigs par ma gyur pa/ /'tsho ba gzhan la mi brten cing/ /chos la chod pa bzhin mi spyad/ /rang gi rnyed pa blang bya zhing/ /gzhan gyi la ni 'dod mi bskyed/ /dge slong
16a1(mdo 'grel): gzhan gyis 'dod byed pa/ /ting 'dzin thob par mi 'gyur ro/ /gal te bde bar 'tsho 'dod cing/ /dge sbyod 'di la lta 'dod na/ /dge 'dun gyi na chos gos dang/ /bza' ltung byin par gyur na blang/ /gal te
16a2(mdo 'grel): bde bar 'tsho 'dod cing/ /dge slong 'di la lta 'dod na/ /byi ba'i khung nas sbrul lta bu/ /gnas mal dag la brten par gyis/ /gal te bde bar 'tsho 'dod cing/ /dge sbyong 'di la lta 'dod na/ /ngan don tsam gyis chog
16a3(mdo 'grel): shes shing/ /chos gcig po yang bsgom par bya/ /gal te mang pos mi shes shing/ /tshul khrims legs par mnyam gzhag na/ /de shes pa dag 'tsho dag cing/ /snyom las med ces bstod par byed/ /gal te 'chi
16a4(mdo 'grel): bdag nyams byed pa'i/ /zag med rig pa gsum ldan na/ /blun po ci yang mi shes zhes/ /bsams nas de la 'phya yang bla/ /gang zag sdig pa'i chos can la/ /gal te bza' dang btung ba yi/ /rnyed pa dag dang ldan gyur
16a5(mdo 'grel): na/ /de la de dag mchod par byed/ /mgo bregs ngur smig gyon pa yis/ /bza' ba dang ni btung ba dang/ /gos dang mal cha rnyed pa ltar/ /dgra byed mang pa kho nar zad/ /de ltar bkur sti 'jigs chen gyis/ /skyon rnams
16a6(mdo 'grel): khong du chud byas nas/ /'phrigs nyung sems khral bskyungs nas su/ /dran ldan dge slong kun tu rgyus/ /kham gyis zas kyis sems zhir mi 'gyur yang/ /'tsho ba 'di phyir mi bza' i mi bya ste/ /kha zas kyis ni lus dag gnas
16a7(mdo 'grel): 'gyur ba/ de ltar rtogs la bsod snyoms dag la rgyus/ /rigs kyis phyag byas mchod pa gang yin 'di/ /zug rngu phra mo dbyung bar dga' ba ste/ /mi yis bzod dga' bkur sti gang yin 'dri/ /'dam dang 'dra bar rab tu
16b1(mdo 'grel): rtogs par gyis/ /bkur sti'i tshoms te bcu gsum pa'o// //sdig pa'i las ni mi byed pa/ /'khu bya min la gang 'khu ba/ /'jig rten 'di dang pha rol tu/ /de nyid sdig pa rnams kyis gos/ /dang por bdag ni phung byed
16b2(mdo 'grel): cing/ /phyin nas gzhan yang phung byed pa/ /khra yi gzan ma'i bya lta bur/ /phung zhing gzhan yang phung byed pa/ /rdeg par byed pas brdeg pa 'thob/ /khon du 'dzin pas khon can mthong/ /de bzhin gshe bas gshe ba ste/ /khro bar
16b3(mdo 'grel): byed la khro ba 'byung/ /'di gzhan dge sbyong byis pa ste/ /dam pa'i chos la mi mkhas pa/ /yongs su tshe thung 'di la yang/ /gyi na'i phyir ni 'khor bar byed/ /'di ni mchog ces bsams nas su/ /so sor sma zhing 'thun 'jug pas/
16b4(mdo 'grel): 'di na dge 'dun 'byed pa'i tshe/ /ci phyir stobs med sems mi byed/ /rus pa gcog cing srog gcod la/ /rta phyugs nor ni 'phrogs pa dang/ /yul 'khor 'joms par byed pa yang/ /phyi nas 'jam du ma byed pa ltar/ /mkhas
16b5(mdo 'grel): pas brtags shing gsungs pa'i tshig /spyod yul ston par byed pa yi/ /chos 'di rnam par shes na go/ khyed cag ci yang byed med 'gyur/ /khyod ni mi mkhas lugs can te/ /kha bye yis ni rtsol byed pa/ /pha rol po dag
16b6(mdo 'grel): mi shes pas/ /bdag ni 'di la brtson par byed/ /'di na mkhas pa gang yin pa/ /de dag bzhams pa'i tshig gis zhi/ /bdag la kha zer bdag la gshe/ bdag pham bdag pham byed pa'o zhes/ /'di gang sems la
16b7(mdo 'grel): 'dzin byed pa/ /de yi kho na ni zhi mi 'gyur/ /bdag la kha zer bdag la ga sha/ bdag pham bdag pham byed pa'o zhes/ /'di gang sems la mi 'dzin pa/ /de yi kho na ni zhi bar 'gyur/ /'di na khon gyis khon can dag /nam
17a1(mdo 'grel): yang zhi bar 'gyur ba med/ /bzod pas khon ni zhi 'gyur ba/ /'di ni chos kyi rang bzhin yin/ /khon gyis khon can nam yang zhi mi 'gyur/ /khon med rnams kyis khon ni zhi bar bya/ /sha khon zhugs pa lus
17a2(mdo 'grel): can la gnod pas/ /de phyir mkhas pas khon par mi bya'o/ /brtan pa legs gnas lhan cig spyad pa yi/ /grogs po mkhas pa gal te rnyed na ni/ /nyon mongs thams cad mngon par zil mnan nas/ /dran ldan dga' ba'i
17a3(mdo 'grel): yid kyis de dang spyad/ /brtan pa legs gnas lhan cig spyad pa yi/ /grogs po mkhas pa gal te ma rnyed na/ /yul 'khor yangs pa spangs pa'i rgyal po ltar/ /gcig pus spyad bya sdig pa mi bya'o/ /bdag dang
17a4(mdo 'grel): mthun par spyod pa yi/ /grogs bzang rnyed par ma gyur na/ /byis pa grogs su mi 'gyur bas/ /gcig pus spyod pa brtan par bya/ /byis pa grogs su mi 'gyur bas/ /gcig pu spyod par byed bla bas/ /ma btang
17a5(mdo 'grel): dgon pa'i glang po ltar/ /sems khral bskyungs te gcig pur spyad/ /'khu ba'i tshoms te bcu bzhi pa'o// //sangs rgyas kyis ni bstan pa bzhin/ /gang zhig dbugs 'byung rdub dran pa/ /yongs su
17a6(mdo 'grel): rdzogs par legs bsgoms pas/ /rim gyis yongs su byang 'gyur te/ /sprin bral nyi ma zla ba ltar/ /'jig rten 'di na kun nas gsal/ /'greng dang 'dug dang de bzhin nyal ba na/ /lus dang de bzhin sems
17a7(mdo 'grel): ni 'jog byed cing/ /dge slong dran pa de legs 'jog pa ni/ /snga phyi'i khyad par rnams ni thob par 'gyur/ /snga phyi'i khyad par rnams ni thob gyur na/ /'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/ /lus rtogs
17b1(mdo 'grel): dran pa nye bar gzhag nas su/ /reg pa'i skye mched drug ni bsdams byas te/ /gang zhig rtag tu mnyam par 'jog byed pa/ /de dag nyid kyis mya ngan 'das pa rtogs/ /gang zhig rtag tu rnam pa thams cad du/ /lus rtogs dran pa nye bar
17b2(mdo 'grel): 'jog byed pa bdag nyid med cing bdag gir 'dzin pa med/ /bdag tu mi 'gyur bdag gir 'dzin mi 'gyur/ /de ltar dge slong mnyam 'jog myur du ni/ /yul la sred pa dag las rgal bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig dran dang shes bzhin
17b3(mdo 'grel): mnyam 'jog dang/ /dga' dang rab tu dang bas dus dus su/ /chos 'di la spyod mel tshe byed pa de/ /skye rga rnams las brgal bar 'gyur zhes gsung/ /de ltas rtag tu mel tshe byed bsten cing/ /dge slong mkhas pa dran ldan
17b4(mdo 'grel): brtson pa yis/ /skye rga'i kun tu sbyor ba spangs nas su/ /des ni 'di la mya ngan 'das pa 'thob/ /gnyid log de dag sad byed pa'i/ /mel tshe dag la khyod nyon cig /nyal bas mel tshe byed bla ste/ /mel tshe byed la 'jigs
17b5(mdo 'grel): ba med/ /mel tshe byed pa brtson pa dang/ /nyin mtshan rjes su slob byed cing/ /'chi ba med la lha ga mos pa'i/ /zag pa rnams ni zad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /sangs rgyas rjes su dran byed cing//
17b6(mdo 'grel): gang dag sangs rgyas skyabs song ba/ /de dag mi yi rnyed pa yin/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /chos rnams rjes su dran byed cing/ /gang dag chos la skyabs song ba/ /de dag mi yi rnyed pa yin/ /gang zhig nyin
17b7(mdo 'grel): dang mtshan rnams su/ /dge 'dun rjes su dran byed cing/ /gang dag dge 'dun skyabs song ba/ /de dag mi yi rnyed pa yin/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /sangs rgyas rjes su dran byed pa/ /
18a1(mdo 'grel): gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /chos rnams rjes su dran byed pa/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad
18a2(mdo 'grel): par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /dge 'dun rjes su dran byed pa/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /tshul khrims
18a3(mdo 'grel): rjes su dran byed pa/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /gtong ba rjes su dran byed pa/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas
18a4(mdo 'grel): sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /lha ni rjes su dran par byed/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /rtag tu lus
18a5(mdo 'grel): rtogs dran byed pa/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /rtag tu ting 'dzin bzhi dran pa/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad
18a6(mdo 'grel): par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /'tshe ba med la yid dga' ba/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /gnod med sems la
18a7(mdo 'grel): yid dga' ba/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /bsgom pa la ni yid dga' ba/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par
18b1(mdo 'grel): 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /stong pa nyid la yid dga' ba/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /mtshan ma med la yid dga' ba/ /
18b2(mdo 'grel): gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /dben pa la ni yid dga' ba/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig
18b3(mdo 'grel): nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /nges par 'byung la yid dga' ba/ /go'u ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /ci yang med la yid dga' ba/ /gau ta ma'i nyan
18b4(mdo 'grel): thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /gang zhig nyin dang mtshan rnams su/ /mya ngan 'das la yid dga' ba/ /gau ta ma'i nyan thos te/ /legs par sad pas sad par 'gyur/ /dran pa'i tshoms te bco
18b5(mdo 'grel): lnga pa'o// //bdag gis bya ba byas pa'i dus g.yo bas/ /dang po kho nar bya ba'i mal tshe gyis/ /bdag gis dang po de ltar byas nas ni/ /bya ba byas pa'i dus lta zad 'dod cing/ /ji ltar 'dod pa de bzhin 'byor
18b6(mdo 'grel): 'gyur bar/ /de yi rang bzhin nga yis mthong bas na/ /ji srid don ni phun sum tshogs 'gyur ba/ /de srid bar du mi yis bsgrim par gyis/ /bsgrim zhing brtson par bya ba yis/ /bdag nyid gling du 'gyur bar bya/ /mgar
18b7(mdo 'grel): ba yis ni dngul bzhin du/ /rang gi dri ma spyad par gyis/ /dri ma spyangs pas skyon mi 'gyur/ /phyi nas skye dang rga mi 'thob/ /ngo tsha min la ngo tsha zhing/ /ngo tsha ba la ngo mi tsha/ /mi 'jigs pa la 'jigs lta dang/ /
19a1(mdo 'grel): 'jigs la mi 'jigs lta ba yi/ /log par lta ba blangs pa yis/ /sems can ngan 'gror 'gro bar 'gyur/ /'di na gang sngon bag med las/ /phyi nas bag dang ldan 'gyur te/ /sprin bral nyi ma zla ba ltar/ /
19a2(mdo 'grel): 'jig rten 'di na kun nas gsal/ /'di na gang sngon bag med las/ /phyi nas bag dang ldan 'gyur te/ /'jig rten 'di na sred pa las/ /dran pas legs par 'da' bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig gzhon nur rab byung nas/ /
19a3(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas bstan la 'jug pa ste/ /sprin bral nyi ma zla ba ltar/ /'jig rten 'di na kun nas gsal/ /gang zhig gzhon nur rab byung nas/ /sangs rgyas bstan la 'jug pa ste/ /'jig rten 'di na sred pa las/ /dran pas
19a4(mdo 'grel): legs par 'da' bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig sdig pa'i las byas pa/ /dge bas 'gegs par byed pa de/ /sprin bral nyi ma zla ba ltar/ /'jig rten 'di na kun nas gsal/ /gang zhig sdig pa'i las byas pa/ /dge bas
19a5(mdo 'grel): 'gebs par byed pa de/ /'jig rten 'di na sred pa las/ /dran pas legs par 'da' bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig gson la mi dga' ba/ /de ni shi na'ang mya ngan med/ /brtan pa go 'phang mthong ba de/ /mya ngan dbus na
19a6(mdo 'grel): gdung mi 'gyur/ /gang zhig gson la mi dga' ba/ /de ni shi na'ang mya ngan med/ /brtan pa go 'phang mthong ba de/ /gnyen 'dun dbus na lam mer 'dug/ /dge slong dkar po bsgom gyis la/ /nag po'i phyogs ni rnam
19a7(mdo 'grel): par spongs/ /khyim nas khyim med song nas su/ /spyod yul dben pa gang yin pa/ /de la mngon par dga' bslab cing/ /'dod pa ci yang med par spongs/ /rtag tu snying po dag pa dang/ /rtag tu gso sbyong dag pa dang/ /
19b1(mdo 'grel): gtsang ma'i las ni dag pa de'i/ /brtul zhugs phun sum tshogs par 'gyur/ /zhing gi skyon na rtswa yin ltar/ /skye dgu 'di la 'dod chags skyon/ /de bas 'dod chags bral rnams la/ /byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/ /zhing gi
19b2(mdo 'grel): skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/ /skye dgu 'di la zhe sdang skyon/ /de bas zhe sdang bral rnams la/ /byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/ /zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/ /skye dgu 'di la gti mug skyon/ /de bas gti mug bral rnams la/ /
19b3(mdo 'grel): byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/ /zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/ /skye dgu 'di la nga rgyal skyon/ /de bas nga rgyal bral rnams la/ /byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/ /zhing gis skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/ /skye dgu 'di la
19b4(mdo 'grel): chags pa skyon/ /de bas chags dang bral rnams la/ /byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/ /zhing gi skyon ni rtswa yin ltar/ /skye dgu 'di la sred pa skyon/ /de bas sred dang bral rnams la/ /byin na 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/ /
19b5(mdo 'grel): drug pa bdag po rgyal po ste/ /chags par gyur na chags can yin/ /ma chags gyur na chags ma yin/ /chags pa byis pa zhes brjod do/ /'dod chags zhe sdang nga rgyal dang/ /'chab pa gang du gnas pa yin/ /grong
19b6(mdo 'grel): khyer rus pa'i ra ba can/ /sha dang khrag gis zhal zhal byas/ /rgyu yis kun nas bslang ba las byung sdug bsngal can/ /de ma mthong na der ni de dag 'ching 'gyur zhing/ /de dag rtogs na chu bo rnams ni rab tu spong/ /phyi rol
19b7(mdo 'grel): pa la chags pa de dag spong ba med/ /sil bu'i tshems te bcu drug pa'o// //de dag khyim la mi dga' bar/ /dran dang ldan pa 'bad pa yis/ /dad pas mtsho ngan spong ba ltar/ /de dag khyim spangs chu bo rgal/ /brtan
20a1(mdo 'grel): pa 'jig rten nges 'byung nas/ /bdud kyi sde rnams rab bcom te/ /nyi ma'i lam nas ngang pa ltar/ /rdzu 'phrul gyis ni mkha' la 'gro/ /tshangs par spyod pa ma spyad cing/ /gzhon nu nor ni ma rnyed pa/ /mtsho ngan nya
20a2(mdo 'grel): nyung dogs dag na/ /chu skyar rgan sems bzhin du 'gyur/ /tshangs par spyod pa ma spyad cing/ /gzhon nu nor ni ma rnyed pa/ /sngan chad byas pa rjes dran pas/ /lus bskums nas ni nyal bar 'gyur/ /sdig pa chung byas bdag
20a3(mdo 'grel): nyid kyis/ /phyi bzhin mi 'ong ma sems shig /chu yi thigs pa ltung ba yis/ /bum chen gang ba ji bzhin du/ /cung zad cung zad bsags pa yi/ /sdig pas byis pa gang bar 'gyur/ /dge ba chung byas bdag nyid kyi/ /phyi
20a4(mdo 'grel): bzhin mi 'ong ma sems shig /chu yi thigs pa ltung ba yi/ /bum chen gang ba ji bzhin du/ /cung zad cung zed bsags pa yi/ /dge bas brtan pa gang bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig rags brtsigs mtsho ngan spangs/ /rgya mtsho'i
20a5(mdo 'grel): chu bo rgal 'dod pa/ /skye bos gzings ni bcas nas kyang/ /skye bo mkhas pa rgyal bar byed/ /brgal nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ /bram ze skam sar gnas par mdzad/ /de la dge slong khrus byed cing/ /nyan thos rnams
20a6(mdo 'grel): kyis gzings kyang bcas/ /ji ltar mtsho chen zab mo dag /rab tu rnam dag rnyeg med ltar/ /de bzhin mkhas pa rab dang bas/ /'di na chos ni nyan par byed/ /'di ltar kun nas chu yod pas/ /su zhig mtsho zhing rgyu byed de//
20a7(mdo 'grel): khron pa chu lta ci zhig dgos/ /sred pa rtsa nas bcad pa'i phyir/ /btso blag mkhan dag chus 'khru zhing/ /mnga' mkhan mes ni srong ba dang/ /shing mkhan shing la 'jog sbyod ltar/ /mkhas pas bdag nyid 'dul bar bya/
20b1(mdo 'grel): nam mkha' lta bur chags med cing/ /sgo thems lta bur g.yo ba med/ /rnyog ma can gyi mtsho lta bur/ /mkhas pa 'khor ba la mi dga' / /chu'i tshoms te bcu bdun pa'o// //lhar bcas gshin rje'i 'jig rten 'di'i
20b2(mdo 'grel): sa stengs las rgyal gang zhig lags/ /me tog lta bur rab 'dod pa'i/ /chos bzhin legs par ston mkha' gang/ /lhar bcas gshin rje'i 'jig rten 'di'i/ /sa stengs las rgyal slob pa yin/ /me tog lta bur rab
20b3(mdo 'grel): 'dod pa'i/ /chos bzhin legs par ston mkhas te/ /nags tshal las ni 'jigs skyes phyir/ /nags tshal bcad kyi shing ma yin/ /nags dang nags sbyor chod cig dang/ /dge slong mya ngan 'da' bar 'gyur/ /gal te
20b4(mdo 'grel): nags sbyor ma bcad na/ /phra rab kyis kyang mi rnams skye/ /ma drung na zho 'dod be'u ltar/ /de yis yid ni rab tu 'ching/ /lag pas ston ka'i pad+ma ltar/ /bdag la dga' ba bcad nas su/ /rgyal gsungs mya ngan 'da' 
20b5(mdo 'grel): ba'i phyir/ /zhi ba'i lam nyid bskyed par gyis/ /ji ltar me tog yid 'ong ba/ /kha dog bzang yang dri med ltar/ /de bzhin legs par gsungs pa'i tshig /'bras bu med par ma byed cig /ji ltar me tog yid 'ong ba/ /
20b6(mdo 'grel): kha dog bzang zhing dri zhim ltar/ /de bzhin legs par gsungs pa'i tshig /'bras bu yod pa nyid du gyis/ /ji ltar bud ba me tog gi /kha dog dri la mi gnod par/ /khu ba bzhibs nas 'phur ba ltar/ /de bzhin
20b7(mdo 'grel): thub pa grong du rgyu/ /gzhan gyi skyon la mi brtag cing/ /gzhan gyi byas dang ma byas min/ /bdag nyid kyis ni rigs pa dang/ mi rigs pa la brtags par bya/ /ji ltar phyag dar phung po dag /mi gtsang chu 'di med
21a1(mdo 'grel): 'di las/ /pad+ma kha bye gtsang ba dang/ /dri zhim yid 'ong rab skyes ltar/ /de bzhin so so'i skye bo dag /ljongs gyur phyag dar pung 'di las/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi nyan thos dag /shes rab kyis ni gsal
21a2(mdo 'grel): 'byung/ /ji ltar ma tog phung po las/ /me tog phreng brgyud mang byed ltar/ /de bzhin mir ni skyes pa yis/ /dge ba phal chen rnams kyang bya/ /ji ltar dbyar ka ba ku la'i/ /me tog rab tu rnam 'brul ltar/ /de
21a3(mdo 'grel): bzhin dge slong 'dod chags dang/ /zhe sdang gti mug spangs par gyis/ /mi yi yid la rnam chags dag /me tog bzhin du rab bsags pa/ /'chi bdag gis ni blangs nas 'gro /nyal grong chu bos pa ngas pa bzhin
21a4(mdo 'grel): mi yi yid la rnam chags dag /me tog bzhin du rab bsags pa/ /'dod pa rnams kyis mi ngoms shing/ /'chi bdag gis ni dbang du byed/ /mi yi yid la rnams chags dag /me tog bzhin du rab
21a5(mdo 'grel): bsags pa/ /longs spyod skye bar mi 'gyur zhing/ /'chi bdag gis ni dbang du byed/ /mi yi yid la rnam chags dag /me tog bzhin du rab bsags pa/ /bya ba mthar ni ma phyin par/ /'chi bdag gis ni
21a6(mdo 'grel): dbang du byed/ /lus 'di bum pa 'dra bar rtogs byas shing/ /de bzhin chos rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/ /bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir spyod pa/ /'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro /'jig
21a7(mdo 'grel): rten 'di dag du ma pa 'drar rtogs shing/ /de bzhin chos rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/ /bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir gcod pa/ /'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/ /lus 'di dbu ba 'dra bar
21b1(mdo 'grel): rtogs byas shing/ /de bzhin ches rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/ /bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir gcod pa/ /'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/ /'jig rten 'di dag dbu pa 'dras rtogs shing/ /de bzhin chos
21b2(mdo 'grel): rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/ /bdud kyi me tog mchog ni 'dir gcod pa/ /'chi bdag rgyal pos bltar yang med par 'gro/ /srid pa u dum bA ra'i me tog ltar/ /snying po med par sems pa'i dge slong gang/ /de ni
21b3(mdo 'grel): pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sprul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/ /chags pa ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sprul
21b4(mdo 'grel): rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/ /zhe sdang ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sprul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /chu skyes rtsa ba'i
21b5(mdo 'grel): me tog chu gnas lta'i/ /gti mug ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sprul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/ /nga rgyal ma lus
21b6(mdo 'grel): gcod byed dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sprul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/ /chags pa ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol
21b7(mdo 'grel): min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sprul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /chu skyes rtsa ba'i me tog chu gnas lta'i/ /sred pa ma lus gcod byed dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sprul rgas
22a1(mdo 'grel): lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /me tog gi tshoms te bco brgyad pa'o// //ji ltar rta bzangs lcag gis bzhus pa na/ /skrag cing shugs drag 'gro byed ji bzhin du/ /dad pa tshul khrims ting
22a2(mdo 'grel): 'dzin ldan pa dang/ /chos rnams rnam par gtan la 'bebs ldan zhing/ /dbang po mnyam gzhag bzod ldan 'grogs bde ba/ /skyob pa de rnams srid pa ma lus spong/ /ji ltar rta bzangs lcag gis bzhus pa na/ /
22a3(mdo 'grel): skrag cing shugs drag 'gro byed ji bzhin du/ /dad pa tshul khrims ting 'dzin ldan pa dang/ /chos rnams rnam par gtan la 'bebs ldan zhing/ /rig dang rkang par ldan zhing drang ldan pa'i/ /skyob rnams sdug bsngal
22a4(mdo 'grel): ma lus spong bar mdzad/ /'dul sbyong byed pas legs btul rta lta bur/ /gang zhig dbang po legs par sdom pa yis khro ba spong zhig zag pa zad byed pa/ /thub de rnams kyis lha'i bar du myong/ /bag yod pa
22a5(mdo 'grel): yis bag med dang/ /mi nyal mang pos gnyid log dang/ /rta bzangs kyis na rta rgod ltar/ /shin tu mkhas pas sbyangs nas 'gro/ /rta bzangs la ni lcags bzhin du/ /gang zhig ngo tsha shes bsten cing/ /shes rab
22a6(mdo 'grel): legs par mnyam gzhag pa/ /des ni sdig pa sel bar byed/ /dul ba mdun sar 'gro byed cing/ /dul ba rgyal po lhag par zhon/ /gang zhig tshig ngan bzod byed dang/ /dul ba mi yi nang na mchog /glang po'i nang na
22a7(mdo 'grel): glang chen dang/ /sin? dul cang shes rta dang ni/ /dre'u 'dul byed gang yin pa/ /de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog /bdag nyid legs 'dul gang yin pa'i/ /mkhas de zhi ba thob 'gyur gyi/ /bzhon pa de dag rnams
22b1(mdo 'grel): kyis ni/ /sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/ /glang po'i nang na glang chen dang/ /sin du'i cang shes ta dang ni/ /dre'u 'dul byed gang yin pa/ /de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog /bdag nyid legs 'dul dran ldan gang/ /des ni sdug
22b2(mdo 'grel): bsngal mthar phyin gyi/ /bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/ /sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/ /glang po'i nang na glang chen dang/ /sin du'i cang shes rta dang ni/ /dre'u 'dul byed gang yin pa/ /de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog /
22b3(mdo 'grel): bdag nyid legs 'dul dran ldan gang/ /des ni 'gro rnams spong 'gyur gyi/ /bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/ /si de mngon par 'thob mi srid/ /glang po'i nang na glang chen dang/ /sin dul cang shes rta dang ni/ /dre'u 'dul
22b4(mdo 'grel): byed gang yin pa/ /de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog /bdag nyid legs 'dul gang yin des/ /'ching pa bcad nas 'gro 'gyur gyi/ /bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/ /sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/ /glang po'i nang na
22b5(mdo 'grel): glang chen dang/ /srin bu'i cang shes rta dang ni/ /dre'u 'dul byed gang yin pa/ /de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog /bdag nyid legs 'dul gang yin nges/ /sdug bsngal kun las rab grol gyi/ /bzhon pa de dag rnams
22b6(mdo 'grel): kyis ni/ /sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/ /glang po'i nang na glang chen dang/ /srin dul cang shes rta dang ni/ /dre'u 'dul byed gang yin pa/ /de bas bdag nyid 'dul ba mchog /bdag nyid legs 'dul gang yin des/ /
22b7(mdo 'grel): kun 'byor ma lus spong 'gyur gyi/ /bzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/ /sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/ /glang po'i nang na glang chen dang/ /srin du'i cang shes rta dang ni/ /dre'u 'dul byad gang yin pa/ /de bas bdag nyid
23a1(mdo 'grel): 'dul ba mchog /bdag nyid legs 'dul gang yin des/ /mya ngan 'das gang 'gro 'gyur gyi/ /gzhon pa de dag rnams kyis ni/ /sa de mngon par 'thob mi srid/ /'dul sbyong byed pa rta bzangs ltar/
23a2(mdo 'grel): bdag nyid kho na 'dul bar bya/ /bdag nyid legs par 'dul ba yis/ /sdug bsngal rnams kyi pha mthar phyin/ /bdag nyid kho na bdag gi mgon/ /bdag nyid bdag gi skyabs yin pas/ /'dul sbyod byed pas
23a3(mdo 'grel): rta bzangs ltar/ /de bas bdag nyid 'dul bar bya/ /rta'i tshoms te bcu dgu pa'o// //khro ba spangs shing nga rgyal rnam spangs na/ /kun sbyor kun las shin tu 'das gyur cing/ /ming dang
23a4(mdo 'grel): gzugs la chags pa med de dag /ci yang med pas chags pas rjes mi ltung/ /skyes ma thag tu khro ba spongs/ /skyes nas 'dod chags spang bar gyis/ /brtan pas ma rig rab tu spang/ /bden pa mthong
23a5(mdo 'grel): bas bde bar 'gyur/ /khro ba spangs nas bde bar nyal/ /khro ba spangs na gdung mi 'gyur/ /dge slong khro ba bde 'joms pa'i/ /dug gi rtsa ba chom zhig dang/ /'phags pa rnams kyis bsngags 'gyur zhing/ /
23a6(mdo 'grel): de bcom pa yis mya ngan med/ /gang khros bdag gis legs byas shing/ /ma legs min zhes rab smra ba/ /de ni khro ba zhi 'og tu/ /me yis bsregs bzhin gdung bar 'gyur/ /ngo tsha med cing khrel med pa/
23a7(mdo 'grel): khro ba can la brtul zhugs med/ /khro bas mngon par zil non pa/ /de la su yang brten mi byed/ /gang zhig byis pa'i mthu stobs can/ /de yi stobs ni stobs med yin pa/ byis pa chos dang bral ba la/ /
23b1(mdo 'grel): bsgrub par bya ba yod re skan/ /gang zhig stobs dang ldan gyur kyang/ /stobs chung rnams kyis bzod byed pa/ /de ni bzod pa'i mchog ces gsungs/ /nyam chung ba lta rtag tu sgur/ /gang zhig gzhan gyi dpon gyur kyang/ /
23b2(mdo 'grel): stobs chung rnams kyis bzod byed pa/ /de ni bzod pa'i mchog ces gsung/ /nyam chung ba lta rtag tu sgur/ /gzhan gyis lhag par brgyad bkag kyang/ /stobs ldan gang zhig bzod byed pa/ /da ni bzod pa'i mchog
