23b4(mdo 'grel): nas/ /bdag nyid nye bar zhi byed pa/ /de ni bdag dang gzhan dag gi /'jigs chen dag las skyob pa yin/ /gang zhig pha rol khros rig nas/ /bdag nyid nye bar zhi byed pa/ /de ni bdag dang gzhan ngag gi /gnyi ga'i
23b5(mdo 'grel): don ni spyod pa yin/ /bdag nyid dang ni gzhan dag dang/ /gnyi ga'i don de spyod de la/ /skye bo chos la mi mkhas rnams/ /phyis pa yin zhes sems kyang bla/ /gtso bo'i tshig ni 'jigs phyir bzod byed dang/ /'thab zla'i
23b6(mdo 'grel): tshig ni 'thab bcugs rgyus bzod pas/ /gang zhig dman pa'i tshig la bzod byed pa/ /bzod pa'i mchog ces dam pas rab tu gsungs/ /byis pa khros nas tshig rtsub dag /smras na rgyal bar 'gyur snyam sems//
23b7(mdo 'grel): gang zhig tshig dag bzod byed pa/ /de ni rtag tu rgyal ba yin/ /bden par smra bya khro mi bya/ /slong la chung yang sbyin par bya/ /rnam pa 'di gsum gnas kyis ni/ /lha yi gnas su 'gro bar 'gyur/ /khro ba'i zil
24a1(mdo 'grel): kyis non pa'i mis/ /rang gi don kyang mi rtogs pas/ /'khor gyi nang du bag skyong la/ /khro ba med pa'i tshig smros shig /gang zhig khros la slar khro ba/ /de ni sdig pa can 'gyur bas/ /khro la slar ni ma
24a2(mdo 'grel): khro dang/ /thub par dka' ba'i yul las rgyal/ /khro ba med pas khro ba thub/ /legs pas legs pa ma yin thub/ /sbyin pa yis ni 'jungs pa thub/ /bde bas bde ba ma yin thub/ /dul zhing rigs pas
24a3(mdo 'grel): 'tsho ba dang/ /khro ba med pas ga la khro/ /yang dag shes pas rnam grol ba'i/ /mkhas pa rnams la khro ba med/ /khro ba med dang 'chi med la/ /'phags pa'i skye bos rtag brten kyang/ /skye bo sdig can khro ba
24a4(mdo 'grel): dag /ri bo bzhin du sgur bar byed/ /gang zhig khro ba byung ba dang/ /shing rta'i 'khyams las 'dzin byed de/ /'dul spyod mkhan du ngas gsungs kyi/ /zhags 'debs skye bo phal pa yin/ /khro ba'i
24a5(mdo 'grel): tshoms te nyi shu pa'o// //sdom la/ dge sbyong lam dang bkur sti dang/ /'khu dang lnga pa dran pa ste/ /sil du chu dang me tog? dang/ /rta dang khro ba bcu pa'o/ /'jig rten 'di na kun zil non/ /'do na chos
24a6(mdo 'grel): rnams kun gyis ma gos shing/ /kun spangs sred zad rab tu rnam grol ba/ /nyid kyis mngon mkhyen pa la su yis bstan/ /de bzhin gshegs pa lha me'i ston pa ste/ /stobs rnams kun ldan thams cad mkhyen pa dang/ /
24a7(mdo 'grel): byang chub bsnyes nas nyid kyis rab ston pa/ /mtshungs med mnyam med nga la su yis bstan/ /nga ni 'jig rten dgra bcom ste/ /'jig rten dag na bla med nga/ /lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten na/ /bdud rnams zil gnan rgyal
24b1(mdo 'grel): ba nga/ /nga dang 'dra ba med pas na/ nga la slob dpon su yang med/ /'jig rten 'di na gcig pu yis/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub bla med brnyes/ /gang zhig zag pa zad brnyes pa/ /rgyal ba nga 'dra shes par gyis/ /sdig pa'i chos las
24b2(mdo 'grel): nga rgyal bas/ /de bas nyer 'gro nga rgyal ba/ /'jig rten yul sred brgal ba yi/ /kun mkhyen sangs rgyas mya ngan 'das/ /'jig rten pa la ma bstan par/ /kun las 'byung ba mi shes pas/ /ba ra NA ser song nas su/ /
24b3(mdo 'grel): ngas ni chos kyi rnga brdung zhing/ /'jig rten sus kyang ma bskor ba'i/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bya/ /dpa' bo de bzhin gshegs pa rnams/ /'di na chos kyis 'dul bar mdzad/ /de dag chos kyi btul ba las/
24b4(mdo 'grel): mkhas bsu yang smod mi byed/ /brtan gang ting 'dzin la zhugs shing/ /nges 'byung zhi la dga' ba dang/ /sku yi tha ma 'dzin pa yi/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas grags ldan pa/ /shes rab myur ba nga dag la/ /lha dang mi
24b5(mdo 'grel): rnams dga' bar byed/ /gang dag 'das pa'i sangs rgyas dang/ /gang dag ma byon sangs rgyas dang/ /gang dag da ltar rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /mang po'i mya ngan sel mdzad pa/ /bzhugs par gyur cing zhugs pa dang/ /de
24b6(mdo 'grel): bzhin bzhugs par 'gyur kun gyis/ /dam chos bla mar mdzad pa 'di/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi chos nyid yin/ /de bas 'di na bdag dga' zhing/ /bdag nyid chen po mngon 'dod pas/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa dran
24b7(mdo 'grel): byas te/ /dam pa'i chos la bla mar bya/ /mi gang sangs rgyas bstan pa la/ /dad pa ma bskyed byis pa de/ /rgud pa'i gnas su 'gro 'gyur te/ /srin mo rnams kyis tshong pa bzhin/ /mi gang sangs rgyas bstan pa la/ /
25a1(mdo 'grel): dad pa bskyed pa shes par can/ /de ni bde bar pha rol 'gro/ /sprin shugs ldan pas tshong pa bzhin/ /de bzhin gshegs pa mnyam med mtshungs pa med/ /bde bar rnam rtog de bzhin rab dben pa'i
25a2(mdo 'grel): rnam rtog gnyis po spyod pa'i sangs rgyas rnams/ /mun bsal pha rol gshegs shing grags dang ldan/ /des ni rnyes bya brnyes shing yid dbang 'gyur/ /kun sgrol zag zad rab tu rnam par grol/ /rnam grol
25a3(mdo 'grel): thugs ldan tha ba zag med rnams/ /lus can 'jig rten rnams la phan phyir gzigs / /gang zhig ri bo'i spo la 'dug nas ni/ /'gro ba rnams la kun tu lta ba ltar/ /de bzhin blo bzang mya ngan bral ba
25a4(mdo 'grel): dag/ chos las byung ba'i khang bzang steng gshegs nas/ /skye bo skye rgas zil non mya ngan gyis/ /gdungs pa rnams la kun tu spyan gzigs nas/ /'chi ba med pa'i sgo mo 'byed mdzad kyis/ /gang dag
25a5(mdo 'grel): nyan 'dod the tshom bsal bar gyis/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshoms te nyi shu gcig pa'o/ //legs par thos dang legs spyod dang/ /khyim nas legs par byung ba dang/ /spong bar byed pas
25a6(mdo 'grel): rab bskor cing/ /dge sbyong gis ni rjes mthun legs/ /byis pa mi mkhas pa dag ni/ /'chi ba med pa lta bur spyod/ /mkhas pa dam pa'i chos de ga la/ /mtshan mo'i nang pa bzhin du byed/ /ji ltar khyim
25a7(mdo 'grel): ni legs g.yogs pa/ /mun pa khebs pa'i nang zhugs na/ /gzugs rnams yod par gyur kyang ni/ /mig ldan bzhin du mi mthong ba/ /de bzhin 'di ni rigs skyes pa'i/ /mi ni blo gros ldan gyur kyang//
25b1(mdo 'grel): sdig pa dang ni dge ba'i chos/ /ma thos bar du shes mi 'gyur/ /mig ldan mar me yod pa yis/ /gzugs rnams mthong ba ji lta bar/ /de bzhin dge dang sdig pa'i chos/ /thos pas rnam par shes par 'gyur/ /
25b2(mdo 'grel): thos pas chos rnams rnam par shes/ /thos pas sdig las ldog par 'gyur/ /thos pas don med spong bar byed/ /thos pas mya ngan 'das pa 'thob/ /gal te thos pa mang gyur yang/ /tshul khrims legs par mi sdom
25b3(mdo 'grel): na/ /de ni tshul khrims phyir smad cing/ /de yi thos pa phun sum min/ /gal te thos pa nyung gyur kyang/ /tshul khrims legs par sdom byed na/ /de ni tshul khrims phyir bsngags shing/ /de yi thos pa phun sum 'gyur//
25b4(mdo 'grel): gang zhig thos pa nyung ba dang/ /tshul khrims legs par mi sdom pa/ /de ni gnyi ka'i phyir smad cing/ /de yi brtul zhugs phun sum min/ /gang zhig mang du thos pa dang/ /tshul khrims legs par sdom byed pa/ /de ni
25b5(mdo 'grel): gnyi ga'i phyir bsngags shing/ /de yis brtul zhugs phun sum 'gyur/ /thos pa mang zhing chos 'dzin dang/ /shes rab ldan zhing mnyam gzhag pa/ /de dag sus kyang smad 'os min/ /dzam+bu'i gling gi gser rgyan
25b6(mdo 'grel): bzhin/ /gang zhig gzugs kyi rjes dpog cing/ /nga la sgra yis 'jal byed pa/ /'dun pa'i 'dod chags ldan pa yi/ /skye bo de yis nga mi shes/ /gal te nang ni rnam shes shing/ /pha rol mthong bar ma gyur na/ /
25b7(mdo 'grel): nang gi 'bras bu mthong ba gang/ /de ni sgra yis drang du rung/ /gal te phyi rol mthong gyur cig/ /nang ni shes par ma gyur na/ /phyi rol 'bras bu mthong ba gang/ /de ni sgra yis drang du rung/ /gal te nang yang mi shes shing/ /
26a1(mdo 'grel): phyi rol mthong bar ma gyur na/ /byis pa kun nas bsgribs pa dag /de ni sgra yis drang du rung/ /gal te nang ni rnam shes shing/ /phyi rol dag kyang mthong gyur pa/ /brtan pa nges 'byung shes rab can/ /de ni sgra
26a2(mdo 'grel): yis drang mi rung/ /rna bas phal cher thos pa dang/ /mig gis mang po mthong na yang/ /brtan pa mthong thos de kun gyis/ /yid ches bya ba mi rigs so/ /legs gsungs thos pa snying por byed pa dang/ /ting nge
26a3(mdo 'grel): 'dzin dag snying por shes gyur kyang/ /gang zhig bag med brlang por byed pa de'i/ /thos dang shes pa don chen mi 'gyur ro/ /gang zhig 'phags pas bstan pa'i chos dga' zhing/ /de bzhin lus dang ngag gis sbyong
26a4(mdo 'grel): byed pa/ /de dag bzod ldan grogs dga' dbang po bsdams/ /thos dang shes pa'i pha rol phyin pa 'thob/ /thos pa'i tshoms te nyi shu gnyis pa'o// //legs par gsungs pa bslab bya zhing/ /dge slong
26a5(mdo 'grel): la ni bsnyen bkur dang/ /dben pa dang ni stan gcig dang/ /sems ni nye bar zhi bar bya/ /stan gcig mal stan gcig pa dang/ /gcig bu snyoms las byed spyod cing/ /gcig pu nags tshal gnas pa dang/ /
26a6(mdo 'grel): gcig pus bdag nyid gdul bar bya/ /gang zhig stong phrag stong dag gi /mi yi g.yul las rgyal ba bas/ /gang zhig bdag las rgyal byed pa/ /de ni mi yi g.yul las rgyal/ /rtag tu sdom pa spyod pa yi/ /
26a7(mdo 'grel): mi yis bdag gdul gcig pu yis/ /bdag nyid las rgyal mchog yin gyi/ /skye dgu gzhan lta phal bar zad/ /shes rab kyis gnas dge slong gis/ /rgyal bar byas la bdud dang ni/ /tshangs par
26b1(mdo 'grel): bcas pas pa mi nus/ /lha yis ma yin dri zas min/ /bdag nyid dang por rigs par gnas byas nas/ /phyi nas bdag gzhan bdag bzhin 'dul bar bya/ /bdag nyid dang por rigs par gnas byas na/ /phyi nas gdul tshe
26b2(mdo 'grel): mkhas pa nyon mi mongs/ /bdag la ji ltar byas pa bzhin/ /gzhan dag la yang de ltar bya/ /bdag nyid dul zhing bde ba yis/ /gzhan dag bde bar 'dul bar bya/ /bdag la ji ltar bya ba bzhin/ /gzhan dag la yang de ltar
26b3(mdo 'grel): bya/ kye ma bdag rang legs 'dul ba/ /bdag nyid dul bas dga' bar 'gyur/ /bdag gi don phyir gzhan don ni/ /mang po dag kyang gtang bar bya/ /bdag don ched cher shes gyur na/ /rang gi don gyi mchog tu gyur / /
26b4(mdo 'grel): bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur ba'i/ /mkhas pas don rnams thob par 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta bu zhig
26b5(mdo 'grel): mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pa'i/ /mkhas pas chos rnams 'thob par 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyis/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pa'i
26b6(mdo 'grel): mkhas pas grags pa thob par 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pa'i/ /mkhas pas bde ba thob par 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi
26b7(mdo 'grel): mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pas/ /mkhas pas bde 'gro thob par 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag
27a1(mdo 'grel): nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pa/ /yun ring mtho ris dga' bar 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pas/ /yun ring gnas
27a2(mdo 'grel): pas dga' bar 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pas/ /gnyen gyi nang na lam mer 'bar/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /
27a3(mdo 'grel): gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pa/ /mya ngan ni phan gdung mi 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon du?
27a4(mdo 'grel): pas/ 'ching ba thams cad gcod par 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pas/ /ngan 'gro thams cad spong bar 'gyur/ /bdag r nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pas/ /sdug bsngal kun las rab tu thar/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon
27a5(mdo 'grel): du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pas/ /bdag nyid mgon du gyur pa 'thob/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon yin gyi/ /gzhan lta su zhig mgon du 'gyur/ /bdag nyid bdag gi mgon gyur pas/ /mya
27a6(mdo 'grel): ngan 'das nyid nye bar 'gyur/ /bdag gi tshoms te nyi shu gsum pa'o// //gang dag don dang mi ldan tshig /tshigs bcad brgya dag smra ba bas/ /gang dag nye bar zhi 'gyur ba'i/ /don ldan tshig gcig
27b1(mdo 'grel): thos pa rung/ /gang dag chos dang mi ldan tshig /tshigs bcad brgya dag smra ba bas/ /gang dag nye bar zhi 'gyur ba'i/ /chos ldan tshig gcig thos pa rung/ /tshul 'chal mnyam par ma bzhag pa/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin
27b2(mdo 'grel): pas/ tshul khrims ldan zhing mnyam gzhag pa/ /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson pa rung/ /brtson spangs le lo ldan pa dag /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /brtson 'grus brtan pa brtsams pa dag /nyin zhag 'ga' 
27b3(mdo 'grel): zhig gson pa rung/ /shes 'chal mnyam par ma bzhag pa/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /shes rab chen po mnyam gzhag pa/ /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson pa rung/ /skye dang 'jig pa ma mthong ba/ /lo brgya
27b4(mdo 'grel): gson pa gang min pas/ /skye dang 'jig par mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson pa rung/ /tshor bzang pa ma mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /tshor ba zad par mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig
27b5(mdo 'grel): gson pa rung/ /zag pa zad pa ma mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /zag pa zad pa mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson pa rung/ /go 'phang mi g.yo ma mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang
27b6(mdo 'grel): yin pas/ /go 'phang mi g.yo mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson pa rung/ /go 'phang lta dka' ma mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /go 'phang lta dka' mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' 
27b7(mdo 'grel): zhig gson pa rung?/ /go 'phang mthon po ma mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /go 'phang mthon po mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson pa rung/ /go 'phang ngam pa ma mthong ba/ /lo
28a1(mdo 'grel): brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /go 'phang dam pa mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson pa rung/ /'chi med go 'phang ma mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /'chi med go 'phang mthong

28a3(mdo 'grel): mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /rdul med go 'phang mthong ba dag /nyin zhag 'ga' zhig gson bar rung/ /rdul bral go 'phang ma mthong ba/ /lo brgyar gson pa gang yin pas/ /rdul bral go 'phang

28a6(mdo 'grel): yin des/ /dam pa'i chos la dad pa yis/ /bcu drug char yang mi phod do/ /zla ba re rer ku sha'i rtses/ /kha zas za ba gang yin des/ /dge 'dun la ni dad pa yis/ /bcu drug char yang mi phod do/ /zla ba re rer ku sha'i
28a7(mdo 'grel): rtses/ kha zas za ba gang yin des/ /sems can rnams la snying rje yi/ /bcu drug char yang mi phod do/ /zla ba re rer ku sha'i rtses/ /kha zas za ba gang yin des/ /srog chags rnams la snying rje ba'i/ /bcu drug char
28b1(mdo 'grel): yang mi phod do/ /zla ba re rer ku sha'i rtses/ /kha zas za ba gang yin des/ /'byung ba rnams la snying brtse ba'i/ /bcu drug char yang mi phod do/ /zla ba re rer ku sha'i rtses/ /kha zas za ba gang yin des/ /byams pa sems par

29a1(mdo 'grel): rten du/ /sbyin sreg mchod sbyin cung zad ci byas des/ /gang zhig drang po'i sems kyis phyag 'tshal ba/ /de yi bcu drug char yang mi phod do/ /sgre ba'i tshoms te nyi shu bzhi pa'o// //
29a2(mdo 'grel): ched du brjod pa'i tshoms so// //bam po gsum pa/ /dad pa med cing 'dzungs pa dang/ /dbyen can phra ma can dag dang/ /mkhas pas shes par mi bya zhing/ /sdig can mi dang 'grogs mi bya/ /dad ldan

29a4(mdo 'grel): dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten bya zhing/ /skyes bu dam pa bsten par bya/ /de lta bu dag bsten byas na/ /sdig par mi 'gyur legs par 'gyur/ /gang dag thos mang gnas mang sems pa dang/ /dad dang shes
29a5(mdo 'grel): rab ldan de mi yis bsten/ /'dir ni de yis legs smras mnyan byas na/ /ring po nas kyang khyad par thob par 'gyur/ /dman pa bsten pas mi dag nyams 'gyur zhing/ /thad kar bab pa bsten pas so na gnas
29a6(mdo 'grel): gtso bo bsten pas dam pa thob 'gyur ba/ /de phyir bdag pas gtsor gyur bsten par bya/ /tshul khrims nye bar zhi ba dang/ /shes rab ches mchog ldan pa yi/ /gtso bo gang yin de bsten na/ /gtso bo bas kyang
29a7(mdo 'grel): ches gtsor 'gyur/ /mi yis 'di na nya rul la/ /ku sha'i gtsang byed bcings pa dag /ku sha nyid kyang rul 'gyur ba/ /sdig pa bsten pa 'ang de bzhin 'gyur/ /mi yis rgya spos pa la sha'i/ /lo mar phur ba byas pa
29b1(mdo 'grel): gang/ lo ma nyid kyang dri zhim pa/ /dam pa bsten pa'ang de bzhin 'gyur/ /gal te sdig pa byed pa dag /sdig mi byed pas bsten na yang/ /sdig pa byed par dogs skye zhing/ /mi snyan pa yang 'phel bar 'gyur/ /bsten bye ma yin
29b2(mdo 'grel): bsten pa'i mi/ /de yi skyon gyis skyon can 'gyur/ /dong par dug bskus mda'i bcug pas/ /dug mi bskus pa'ang gos pa bzhin/ /brtan pa skyon gos 'jigs pa dag /sdig pa can dag bshes mi bya/ /ji ltar
29b3(mdo 'grel): grogs po bsten pa dang/ /ji ltar nye bar bstan byas pa/ /bstan bya de ni ci 'dra bar/ /ring por mi thogs de 'drar 'gyur/ /de bas 'bras bu'i snod bzhin du/ /bdag gis bsten pa shes pa yis/ /dam pa ma yin
29b4(mdo 'grel): mi bsten cing/ /mkhas pas dam pa bsten byas la/ /dge slong de lam rjes 'brangs na/ /sdug bsngal zad pa thob par 'gyur/ /byis pa ji srid gson par du/ /gal te mkhas pa bsten byas kyang/ /de yis chos shes
29b5(mdo 'grel): mi 'gyur te/ /gzar bus tshod ma'i ro bzhin no/ /shes rab ldan pas yud tsam zhig /mkhas pa nye bar bsten pas kyang/ /de yis chos rnams shes 'gyur te/ /lce yis tshor ma'i re bzhin no/ /byis pa ji srid
29b6(mdo 'grel): gson par du/ /gal te mkhas pa bsten byas kyang/ /de la mig ni med pa'i phyir/ /chos rnams shes par mi 'gyur ro/ /shes rab ldan pas yud tsam zhig /mkhas pa nye bar bsten byas kyang/ /de la mig ni
29b7(mdo 'grel): yod pa'i phyir/ /chos rnams rab tu shes par 'gyur/ /byis pa ji srid gson par du/ /gal te mkhas pa bsten byas kyang/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa yi/ /chos rnams de yis shes mi 'gyur/ /shes
30a1(mdo 'grel): rab ldan pas yud tsam zhig /mkhas pa nye bar bsten byas kyang/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa'i/ /chos rnams de yis shes par 'gyur/ /don ldan tshig ni gcig gis kyang/ /mkhas pa yi ni bya ba byed//
30a2(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung gis kyang/ /byis pa'i bya ba byed mi 'gyur/ /blo dang ldan pa'i tshig gcig gis/ /tshig brgya dag ni shes 'gyur gyi/ /byis pa dag gi tshig stong gis/ /tshig gcig shes par mi 'gyur ro/ /
30a3(mdo 'grel): nyis na mkhas dang mi mdza' bla'i/ /byis pa rnams dang mdza' mi rung/ /byis pa rnams dang mdza' byed pa/ /sems can dmyal bar khrid par byed/ /byis pa gang zhig byis pa'o zhes/ /shes pa de 'dir mkhas pa yin/ /
30a4(mdo 'grel): byis pa gang zhig mkhas sems pa/ /de ni byis pa zhes brjod do/ /byis pa bstod pa gang yin dang/ /mkhas pas smad pa gang yin las/ /mkhas pas smad pa ches rung gi /byis pas bstod pa mi rung ngo/ /byis pa
30a5(mdo 'grel): bstod pas sdug bsngal zhing/ /rnam pa kun tu dgrar 'dra bas/ /byis pa mi thos mi mthong zhing/ /mi bsten gyur pa nyid rung ngo/ /gnyen dang phrad pa ji lta bas/ /brtan pa bsten na bde bar 'gyur/ /de bas rgyu skar lam du
30a6(mdo 'grel): zla ba ltar/ /brtan zhing thos mang mchog 'dren byed pa dang/ /tshul khrims ldan dang 'phags pa'i brtul zhugs can/ /mi mchog brtse ldan blo bzang bsten par gyis/ /mdza' bshes kyi tshoms te nyi shu
30a7(mdo 'grel): lnga pa'o// //ru sbal rang gi khog par yan lag ltar/ /dge slong yid kyi rnam rtog nang bsdus nas/ /brten pa med cing gzhan la 'tshe med par/ /mya ngan 'das la su yang smos mi byed/ /bzod pa dka' 
30b1(mdo 'grel): thub mchog ste bzod pa ni/ /mya ngan 'das pa mchog ces sangs rgyas gsung/ /rab tu byung ba gzhan la 'tshe ba ni/ /gzhan la gnod pas dge sbyong ma yin no/ /tshig rtsub ci yang smra mi bya/ /smras na yang yang smra bar byed/ /'thab spugs
30b2(mdo 'grel): tshig gis sdug bsngal zhing/ /de la phyir yang chad pas gcod/ /gal te bdag gis bar byas na/ /khar ba'i snod la brdungs pa bzhin/ /'khor bar skye dang rga ba dag /yun rings nyams su myang bar 'gyur/ /bdag gis
30b3(mdo 'grel): phar ni ma byas dang/ /khar ba'i snod las ma brdungs ltar/ /'di ltar 'thab mo mi 'byung zhing/ /mya ngan 'das pa thob par 'gyur/ /nad med rnyed pa'i dam pa ste/ /chog shes pas ni nor gyi dbyig /yid gcugs bshes
30b4(mdo 'grel): pa'i mchog yin te/ /mya ngan 'das pa bde ba'i phul/ /'du byed sdug bsngal ma rung ba/ /nad kyi nang na bkres mi bzang/ /de ltar ji bzhin shes na ni/ /mya ngan 'das pa mchog tu 'gyur/ /bde 'gror 'gro ba nyung zad de/ /
30b5(mdo 'grel): ngan 'gror 'gro ba bsams yas shing/ /de ltar nyes dmigs rtogs gyur na/ /myur du mya ngan 'das pa 'thob/ /bde 'gror 'gro ba rgyu dang bcas/ /ngan 'gror 'gro ba rgyu dang ldan/ /mya ngan 'das 'gro rgyu can de/ /de
30b6(mdo 'grel): dag thams cad rgyu dang bcas/ /nags tshal mchog tu ri dags 'gro/ /mkha' la bya rnams 'gro bar byed/ /chos la rnam par bsgoms 'gro ste/ /dgra bcom mya ngan 'das par 'gro/ /'di ni brtson 'grus zhan
30b7(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ /blo chung shes pa med pa yis/ /mdud pa thams cad rab gtugs pa'i/ /mya ngan 'das ba thob mi 'gyur/ /khyed kyis gru 'di chu phyogs dang/ /'di ni yang bar 'gyur ba ltar/ /de bzhin zhe sdang 'dod chags
31a1(mdo 'grel): spongs/ /de nas mya ngan 'das pa 'thob/ /sngon chad byung ba mi 'byung zhing/ /ma byung ba dag 'byung bar 'gyur/ /ma byung 'byung bar mi 'gyur la/ /da ltar byung ba'ang yod ma yin/ /blta dka' mdza' med bde
31a2(mdo 'grel): med mthong/ /bden pa rab rtogs shes pa dang/ /sred dang dga' ba med mthong ba/ /'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mdza' / /sred pa rnams ni bcang ba dang/ /'dod chags rab tu spangs pa dang/ /mtsho skams nas ni mi 'bab
31a3(mdo 'grel): pa/ 'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mdza' / /lus zhig tshor ba bsil bar 'gyur/ /'du shes 'gags shing 'du byed zhi/ /rnam par shes pa nub gyur pa/ /'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mdza' / /lta bas mthong bar gyur
31a4(mdo 'grel): tsam dang/ /nyan pas thos par gyur pa tsam/ /rtog par byed pas rtogs tsam dang/ /rnam par shes pas rnam shes tsam/ /'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mdza' / /'di dang ma dad gdungs rab gdungs/ /'di 'dra 'di ni
31a5(mdo 'grel): sdug bsngal mdza' / /ma reg ma dga' rab zhi dang/ /kun tu 'dod chags bral gyur pa/ /'di 'dra 'di ni sdug bsngal mdza' / /brten pa yod pas spyod par 'gyur/ /spyod pa yod pas gzhol bar 'gyur/ /gzhol ba yod
31a6(mdo 'grel): pas shin tu ma sbyangs par 'gyur ro/ /shin tu ma sbyangs pa yod pas 'gro ba dang 'ong bar 'gyur ro/ /'gro ba dang 'ong ba yod pas gzhan du 'chi 'pho len par 'gyur ro/ /gzhan du 'chi 'pho blangs pas 'di ltar gzhan du
31a7(mdo 'grel): skye ba dang/ /rga ba dang na ba dang 'chi ba dang mya ngan dang/ /smre sngags 'don pa dang/ /sdug bsngal ba dang/ /yid mi bde ba dang/ /'khrug pa 'byung zhing 'di ltar sdug bsngal gyi phung po 'ba' zhig pa 'di 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /
31b1(mdo 'grel): brten pa med pas spyod pa med par 'gyur ro/ /spyod pa med pas gzhol bar mi 'gyur ro/ /gzhol bar ma gyur pas shin tu sbyangs par 'gyur ro/ /shin tu sbyangs pas 'gro ba dang 'od bar mi 'gyur ro/ /'gro ba dang 'ong bar ma gyur pas
31b2(mdo 'grel): gzhan du 'chi 'pho len par mi 'gyur ro/ /gzhan du 'chi 'pho len pa med pas/ /'di ltar gzhan du skye ba dang/ rga ba dang/ na ba dang/ 'chi 'pho dang/ mya ngan dang/ smre sngags 'don pa dang/ /sdug bsngal ba dang/ yid mi bde ba
31b3(mdo 'grel): dang/ 'khrug pa rnams 'gags par 'gyur zhing/ /'di ltar sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po 'ba' zhig 'di 'gag par 'gyur ro/ /dge slong dag ma skyes pa dang/ ma byung ba dang/ ma bcos pa dang/ 'dus ma byas pa dang/ mi
31b4(mdo 'grel): 'byung ba yod do/ /skye ba dang 'byung ba dang bcos ma dang sems pas byas pa dang 'dus byas pa dang/ /rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yod do/ /dge slong ngag gal te ma skyes pa dang/ ma byung ba dang ma bcos pa dang 'dus ma byas dang/
31b5(mdo 'grel): mi 'byung ba med du zin na skye ba dang 'byung ba dang bcos ma dang/ 'dus byas pa dang/ sems pas byas pa dang/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i nges par 'byung ba yod do zhes nga mi smra'o/ /dge slong dag gang gi phyir 'di na ma
31b6(mdo 'grel): skyes pa dang/ ma byung ba dang/ ma bcos pa dang 'dus ma byas pa dang mi 'byung ba yod pa de'i phyir skye ba dang 'byung ba dang/ bcos ma dang 'dus byas dang sems pas byas pa dang/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i nges par
31b7(mdo 'grel): 'byung ba yod do/ /zhes nga smra'o/ /skye dang byung dang 'byung ba dang/ /bcos dang 'dus byas mi brtan zhing/ /rga dang 'chi dang rmongs pa yi/ /chos can rab tu 'jug 'gyur ba/ /zas kyi rgyu las byung ba yi/ /'jig 'gyur
32a1(mdo 'grel): 'di la dga' mi bya/ /de yi nges par 'byung ba'i gzhi/ /rtog dang dpyod dang zhi ba dang/ /sdug bsngal chos rnams 'gags pa ste/ /'du byed nye bar zhi bar bde/ /dge slong dag de ni gang du yang gnas par mi 'gyur te//
32a2(mdo 'grel): sa la gnas par mi 'gyur/ chu la ma yin me lam yin rlung la ma yin/ nam mkha' mdza' yas skye mched la ma yin/ /rnam shes mdza' yas skye mched la ma yin/ /ci yang med pa'i skye mched la ma yin/ /'du
32a3(mdo 'grel): shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la ma yin/ /'jig rten 'di la ma yin/ /'jig rten pha rol la ma yin/ /nyi ma dang zla ba gnyis la gnas pa ma yin te/ /'di la dmigs pa med par ngas mngon par shes so/ /
32a4(mdo 'grel): dge slong dag de la 'gro ba dang 'ong ba yod par nga mi smra ste/ /gnas par ma yin no/ 'chi 'pho yod par nga mi smra ste/ gnas par ma yin no/ /'chi 'pho yod par nga mi smra ste/ skye bar ma yin pa 'di lta bu ni sdug bsngal
32a5(mdo 'grel): gyi mdza' yin no/ /sa dang chu dang me dang rlung/ /gang la'ang gnas pa ma yin pa/ /de la dkar pos gsal mi byed/ /de la mun pa'ang yod ma yin/ /de la zla bas snang mi byed/ /de la nyi mas mngon mi byed/ /thub pa bram
32a6(mdo 'grel): ze gang yin pa/ /de ni rang gis rig pa yin/ /des ni gzugs dang gzugs med dang/ /sdug bsngal kun las rab tu 'grol/ /mthar phyin 'jigs pa med pa ste/ /rlom med 'gyod pa med pa yin/ /srid pa'i zug rngu
32a7(mdo 'grel): gtugs pa ste/ /lus kyi tha mar gyur pa yin/ /'di ni mthar phyin rnams kyi mchog /zhi ba'i go 'phang bla med pa/ /mtshan ma thams cad zad pa ste/ /byang grol go 'phang 'chi med yin/ /mtshungs dang mi mtshungs
32b1(mdo 'grel): byung ba yi/ /'du byed thub pas rab tu spangs/ /nang du mnyam gzhag dga' ba yis/ /sgo nga'i spubs ni dral nas byung/ /sbyin kun chos kyi sbyin pas thub/ /dga' kun chos kyi dga' bas thub/ /stobs kun bzod pa'i stobs kyis thub
32b2(mdo 'grel): bde kun srad pa zad pas thub/ /mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshoms te nyi shu rtsa drug pa'o// //bdag las gzhan pa'i skyon dag ni/ /phub ma gtor ba ji bzhin du/ /gzhan gyi skyon mthong sla ba ste/ /rang gi skyon ni mthong
32b3(mdo 'grel): bar dka' / /g.yon can tshe long 'jo ba ltar/ /rang gi de ni sped pa dang/ /gzhan gyi skyon la lta byed cing/ /rtag tu 'phyas long 'du shes can/ /de yis ring du chos mi mthong/ /g.yon phyogs chos ni rab tu 'phel/ /spyi
32b4(mdo 'grel): brtol byed cing 'phrogs rlom can/ /mi gtsang las ldan khwa lta bu/ /shin tu nyon mongs 'tsho ba can/ /ngo tsha med pa'i 'tsho ba sla/ /rtag tu gtsang ma 'tshol ba dang/ /thub khyod mi byed 'dzem bag can/ /'tsho ba dag la lta
32b5(mdo 'grel): ba yi/ /ngo tsha shes pa'i 'tsho ba dka' / /'jig rten mun par gyur 'di ste/ /de las lhag mthong ldan pa nyung/ /rgya las shor ba'i bya lta bur/ /mtho ris la dga' shes tsam zhig /byis pa las kyis bcings gyur pa/ /mun
32b6(mdo 'grel): pa'i 'khor gyis bskor ba yin/ /'jig rten nor la chags pa dag /gzhan rdzas lta bur lta bar byed/ /bdag gi skye dgu 'di phyung zhing/ /gzhan gyis byas so snyam sems pa/ /bden pa min la bden lta bas/ /ci yang
32b7(mdo 'grel): mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/ /de ni 'gas kyang mi mthong zhing/ /zug rngu mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/ /yul sred gang la skye bo chags pa yi/ /zug rngu de dag mngon chad mthong ba gang/ /de ni bdag gis byas snyam mi 'dzin cing//
33a1(mdo 'grel): de ni gzhan gyis byas snyam mi 'dzin to/ /skye dgu 'di dag nga rgyal ldan/ /nga rgyal la chags nga rgyal bcings/ /brtsod par gyur pa'i lta ba can/ /'khor ba ldog par mi 'gyur ro/ /thob par gyur pa gang
33a2(mdo 'grel): yin dang/ /thob par bya ba gang yin pa/ /de dag gnyi ga rdul gyis yogs/ /rjes su nad pa slob par byed/ /gang zhig tshul khrims dang/ bslab pa dang brtul zhugs dang/ tshangs par spyod pa dang/ /dka' thub dang/ nye bar
33a3(mdo 'grel): gnas pa snying por byed pa 'di ni mdza' gcig go /gang zhig de ltar blta zhing 'di skad ces 'dod pa ni gtsang ba'o/ /'dod pa ni bsod snyoms can no/ /'dod pa ni longs spyad par bya ba'o/ /'dod pa ni skyon med pa yin
33a4(mdo 'grel): no zhes smra zhing/ /de dag lhag par 'dod pa rnams su ltung bar byed pa'i brtul zhugs len pa 'di yang mdza' gcig go /mdza' gnyis po 'di dag ni dur khrod 'phel bar byed pa ste/ /'di dag gis dur khrod 'phel bar
33a5(mdo 'grel): byas so/ /mdza' gnyis po 'di dag ma mthong ba kha cig zhen par byed la/ /kha cig mngon par rgyug par byed cing/ /de dag lhag par zhen par byed la/ /lhag par rgyug par byed pa dag mig dang ldan pas mthong ngo/ /
33a6(mdo 'grel): mdza' gnyis po de dag mthong ba na zhen par mi byed/ /rgyug par mi byed la/ /de dag lhag par mi byed cing/ /lhag par rgyug par mi byed pa yang mig dang ldan pas mthong ngo/ /de dag de ltar mi byed cing de dag de ltar
33a7(mdo 'grel): mi sems na/ de dag gi lam du mi gdags pa 'di lta bu 'di ni sdug bsngal gyi mdza' yin no/ /ji ltar chu bur mthong ba dang/ /ji ltar smig rgyu mthong ba ltar/ /de bzhin 'jig rten lta byed pa/ /'chi bdag rgyal pos
33b1(mdo 'grel): mthong mi 'gyur/ /ji ltar chu bur mthong ba dang/ /ji ltar smig rgyu mthong ba ltar/ /de bzhin lus la lta byed pa/ /'chi bdag rgyal pos mthong mi 'gyur/ /gang la byis pa mngon chags pa/ /de la mkhas pa chags mi 'gyur//
33b2(mdo 'grel): rgyal po'i shing rta bkra ba ltar/ /lus ni rtag tu blta par gyis/ /gang la byis pa rmongs 'gyur pa/ /de la mkhas pa rmongs mi 'gyur/ /rgyal po'i shing rta bkra ba ltar/ /lus 'di rtag tu blta bar gyis/ /gang du byis pa
33b3(mdo 'grel): nyams gyur pa/ /glang rgan rdzab tu chud pa bzhin/ /rgyal po'i shing rta blta ba ltar/ /lus 'di rtag tu blta bar gyis/ /nang pa lta bur 'jigs chos can/ /rma byung ba dang 'dra ba ste/ /gang yang brtan par mi
33b4(mdo 'grel): gnas par/ /lus 'di rtag tu blta bar gyis/ /nad pa 'jig pa'i chos can ltar/ /gang yang brtan par mi gnas par/ /nor bu'i rna cha gdub 'khor gyis/ brgyan pa'i lus la blta bar gyis/ /skra ni lan bu brgyan
33b5(mdo 'grel): byas shing/ /mig sman gyis ni bskus pa'i mig /byis pa lhag par rmongs byed kyang/ /pha rol tshol bar mi byed do/ /mig sman gyis ni gsar bris shing/ /rnag can lus ni brgyan pa yis/ /byis pa lhag par rmongs
33b6(mdo 'grel): byed kyang pha rol tshol bar mi byed do/ /lus ni dri zhim gyis bskus nas/ /rkang pa btsags gis byugs pa dag /byis pa lhag par rmongs byed kyang/ /pha rol tshol bar mi byed do/ /gang zhig 'dod par kun sbyor 'brel
33b7(mdo 'grel): chags shing/ /kun tu sbyor ba'i skyon rnams ma mthong ba/ /'dod par 'brel la chags pa'i mi de yis/ /chu bo mdza' yas yangs la rgal mi 'gyur/ /chags bral mchog dang tha ma thams cad dag /'di la
34a1(mdo 'grel): bdag dang bdag gir mi lta zhing/ /de dag rnam grol sngon chad ma rgal pa'i/ /chu bo rab brgal yang srid med par 'gyur/ /gang zhig tshal spangs tshal med pa/ /nags tshal spangs nas nags su rgyug /grol ba
34a2(mdo 'grel): 'ching bar rgyug pa yi/ /gang zag 'di la ltos shig tshur/ /shing rta mthun pa'i rtsibs ldan pa/ /yan lag yid 'ong gos dkar g.yogs/ /sdig med 'gro ba la ltos la/ /chings ma'i rgyun rnams bcad par gyis/ /'jigs
34a3(mdo 'grel): pas skrag pa'i mi dag ni/ /phal cher ri dang nags tshal dang/ /skyed mos tshal dang mtsho gnas dang/ /ljon shing rnams la skyabs su 'gro/ /skyabs de gtso bo ma yin zhing/ /skyabs de mchog tu gyur pa min/ /de la skyabs
34a4(mdo 'grel): su song ba yis/ /sdug bsngal kun las grol mi 'gyur/ /gang zhig sangs rgyas chos dang ni/ /dge 'dun la ni skyabs song zhing/ /sdug bsngal sdug bsngal kun 'byung dang/ /sdug bsngal yang dag 'das pa dang/ /bde ba mya ngan
34a5(mdo 'grel): 'das 'gro ba'i/ /'phags lam yan lag brgyad pa ste/ /'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag /gang tshe shes rab kyis mthong ba/ /de ni skyabs kyi mchog yin zhing/ /de ni skyabs kyi dam pa yin/ /de la skyabs su song ba
34a6(mdo 'grel): yis/ sdug bsngal kun las grol bar 'gyur/ /mthong bas mthong zhing mthong bas mi mthong mthong/ /ma mthong mi mthong mthong bya mthong mi 'gyur/ /'dra mthong lhag mthong tha dad dngos por brjod/ /nyin mtshan nam yang
34a7(mdo 'grel): lhan cig mi gnas bzhin/ /'dra ba mthong bas mthong mi 'gyur/ /gal te mthong na 'dra ma mthong/ /mthong 'dis 'dra ba mi mthong ste/ /'dra mthong mi yis mthong ba med/ /mi yis ci ma mthong na 'dra ba mthong/ /
34b1(mdo 'grel): ci zhig mthong na 'dra ba mthong mi 'gyur/ /ji ltar 'di na 'dra ba mthong ba dag /gang zhig med na 'dra bar mthong dang bral/ /gang tshe 'di yis sdug bsngal ma mthong ba/ /de yi tshe na bdag tu mthong bar 'gyur/ /ji lta ji ltar sdug bsngal rtogs
34b2(mdo 'grel): gyur pa/ /des na bdag ni 'dra ba mthong mi 'gyur/ /gang zhig so so'i skye bsgribs nas/ /'du byed sdug bsngal ma mthong ba/ /de phyir 'di na 'dra mthong ste/ /de med 'dra ba mi mthong ngo/ /mthong ba'i tshoms te nyi shu bdun pa'o// //
34b3(mdo 'grel): sdig pa thams cad mi bya ste/ /dge ba phun sum tshogs par spyad/ /rang gi sems ni yongs su gdul/ /'di ni sangs rgyas bstan pa yin/ /sbyin pas bsod nams rab tu 'phel/ /legs bsdams dgra sogs mi 'gyur ro/ /dge
34b4(mdo 'grel): dang ldan pas sdig pa spong/ /nyon mongs zad pas mya ngan 'das/ /mkhas dang 'dre dang byis pa'i skye bo dang/ /lhan cig spyod dang gcig phu gnas kyang rung/ /ngang? pas chu las 'o ma mthung ba ltar/ /mkhas pas sdig pa can rnams
34b5(mdo 'grel): rab tu spangs/ /'jig rten nyes dmigs mthong ba dang/ /'gog par 'gyur ba'i chos mthong bas/ /'phags pa sdig la dga' mi byed/ /sdig can dge la dga' mi 'gyur/ /legs par nya zhi'i ro dang ni/ /rab tu dben
34b6(mdo 'grel): pa'i ro shes pa/ /rims nad med cing sdig med la/ /chos la dga' ba'i ro dag 'thung/ /sems kyi zag pa med pa dang/ /sems ni 'chid bas ma bcos la/ /dge dang sdig pa rab spangs pa/ /ngan 'gro rnams kyi 'jigs
34b7(mdo 'grel): pa med/ /gnas min zlog dang legs smra dang/ /nyes dmigs ston par byed pa dang/ /mkhas pa tshar gcod smra byed pa/ /de lta'i skye dgu bsten par bya/ /de lta bu dag bsten byas na/ /sdig par mi 'gyur legs par 'gyur//
35a1(mdo 'grel): nye bar zhi zhing rab zhi la/ /dal bus smra zhing khengs med pa/ /sdig pa'i chos rnams sprug byed de/ /rlung gis ljon shing lo ma bzhin/ /gang zhig skye dgu dag cing nyon mongs med/ /rab tu sdang med mi la khro byed pa'i
35a2(mdo 'grel): byis pa de la sdig pa phyir mgo ste/ /rdzi phyogs su ni rdul rnams gtong ba bzhin/ /dge ba byed pas dge ba dang/ /sdig pa byed pas sdig pa ste/ /mi yis gang dang gang byas pa/ /de de rang gi mthong bar 'gyur/ /bdag gis
35a3(mdo 'grel): sdig pa byas na ni/ /de bdag kho na kun nyon mongs/ /bdag gis sdig pa ma byas na/ /bdag nyid kho na rnam par dag /gzhan gyis gzhan sbyor mi byed kyi/ /dag dang ma dag rang rang byed/ /bdag nyid kyis ni sdig pa
35a4(mdo 'grel): dag /byas shing nye bar bsams pa yi/ /bsam brlag mngon du 'joms par byed/ /rdo rjes nor bu 'bigs pa bzhin/ /mig ldan 'gro bar byed pa yis/ /nyam nga'i lam dag ji lta bar/ /mkhas pas 'tsho ba'i 'jig
35a5(mdo 'grel): rten 'dir/ /sdig pa dag ni yongs su spangs/ /nor chen gyis ni grogs nyung dang/ /tshong pas 'jigs bcas lam dang ni/ /gson par 'dod pas dug lta bur/ /mkhas pas sdig pa yongs su spang/ /gal te lag mthil
35a6(mdo 'grel): rma med na/ /lag pas dug ni bzung byas kyang/ /rma med dug ni mi 'dzin ltar/ /ma byas pa la sdig pa med/ /bdag la mi phan bya ba dang/ /legs pa ma yin bya bar sla/ /gang dag phan zhing bde 'gyur ba/ /de ni mchog tu bya
35a7(mdo 'grel): bar dka' / /dam pas legs par byas la yi/ /dam pas sdig pa bya bar dka' / /ngan pas sdig pa bya sla yi/ /'phags pas sdig pa bya bar dka' / /ji srid sdig pa ma smin pa/ /de srid byis pa mngar bar sems/ /gang tshe
35b1(mdo 'grel): sdig pa smin gyur pa/ /de tshe de ni tsha bar sems/ /ji srid sdig pa ma smin pa/ /de srid srid pa rung bar blta/ /gang tshe sdig pa smin gyur pa/ /de tshe sdig par mthong bar 'gyur/ /ji srid bzang po ma smin par/ /de srid bzang po dman par mthong//
35b2(mdo 'grel): gang tshe bzang por smin gyur pa/ /gang tshe bzang por mthong bar 'gyur/ /sdig pa sdug bsngal stsogs pas na/ /de la dga' bar mi bya'o/ /brgyal sdig pa byas na yang/ /yang dang yang du de mi bya/ /bsod nams bde ba sogs pas
35b3(mdo 'grel): na/ de nyid la ni dga' bar bya/ /gal te bsod nams byas na yang/ /de ni yang dang yang du bya/ /sdig la yid ni mngon dga' ba/ /bsod nams dal bus byed 'gyur bas/ /sdig pa la ni sems zlog cing/ /bsod nams
35b4(mdo 'grel): mngon par myur te bya/ /sdig pa chung ngu byas pas kyang/ /'jig rten pha rol 'jigs chen dang/ /phung khrol chen po byed 'gyur te/ /khong par song ba'i dug bzhin no/ /bsod nams chung ngu byas pas kyang/ /'jig rten pha rol bde
35b5(mdo 'grel): ba 'dren/ /don chen dag kyang byed 'gyur te/ /'bru rnams phun sum 'byor ba bzhin/ /gang zhig nyes med chad pas gcod/ /sdang ba min la rab sdang ba/ /gnas gzhan gang yang rung ba bcu/ /myur du thob pa kho nar 'gyur/ /
35b6(mdo 'grel): tshod pa mi bzad pa dag gam/ /yang na lus ni 'dral ba 'am/ /gnod pa'i tshor ba tsha ba 'ang rung/ /yang na sems 'khrug thob par 'gyur/ /gnyen 'dun rnams dang bral ba 'am/ /longs spyod zad par 'gyur ba 'am/ /rgyal
35b7(mdo 'grel): po'i gnod pa 'byung ba 'am/ /mi snyan shin tu mi bzad dam/ /yang na khyim de me chen pos/ /nges par sred par byed par 'gyur/ /shes rab 'chal pa lus zhig nas/ /bcu pa ngan 'gror 'gro bar 'gyur/ /sdig pa byas pas
36a1(mdo 'grel): bag dbab mi bya ste/ /ring byas rgyang mar byas kyang bag mi dbab/ /dben par byas kyang bab? dbab mi bya ste/ /de yi rnam smin yod pas bag mi dbab/ /bsod nams byas pas bag ni dbab bya ste/ /ring byas rgyang ring byas kyang bag dbab
36a2(mdo 'grel): cing/ dben par byas kyang bag ni dbab par bya/ /de yi rnam smin yod pas bag dbab po/ /bdag gis sdig pa byas pas mya ngan byed/ /ring dang rgyang ring byas pas mya ngan byed/ /bdag gis dben par byas pas mya ngan byed/ /de
36a3(mdo 'grel): yi rnam smin yod pas mya ngan byed/ /bdag nyid nag po'i las dang ldan mthong nas/ /'dir yang mya ngan gzhan duAng mya ngan byed/ /sdig pas byas pas gnyi gar mya ngan byed/ /de ni mya ngan de rab mya ngan byed/ /bdag gis
36a4(mdo 'grel): bsod nams byas pas dga' bar 'gyur/ /ring dang rgyang ring byas pas 'ga' bar 'gyur/ /bdag gis dben par byas pas dga' bar 'gyur/ /de yi rnam smin yod pas dga' bar 'gyur/ /bdag nyid rnam dag las

36a6(mdo 'grel): zhing/ ring byas rgyang ring byas pas gdung bar 'gyur/ /bdag gis dben par byas pas gdung 'gyur zhing/ /de yi rnam smin yod pas gdung bar 'gyur/ /bdag nyid nag po'i las dang ldan mthong nas/ /'di na gdung
36a7(mdo 'grel): 'gyur/ pha rol gdung bar 'gyur/ /sdig pa byas pas gnyi gar gdung 'gyur zhing/ /de ni gdung 'gyur de rab gdung bar 'gyur/ /bdag gis bsod nams byas pas dga' 'gyur zhing/ /ring byas rgyang ring byas pas dga' /
36b1(mdo 'grel): bar 'gyur/ /bdag gis dben par byas pas dga' 'gyur zhing/ /de yi rnam smin yod pas dga' bar 'gyur/ /bdag nyid dkar po'i las dang ldan mthong nas/ /'di na dgar 'gyur pha rol dga' bar 'gyur/ /bsod nams byas
36b2(mdo 'grel): bas gnyi gar dgar 'gyur zhing/ /de ni gar 'gyur de rab dga' bar 'gyur/ /sdig pa byas shing bsod nams ma byas la/ /chos dang gol zhing chos min thob ma'i mi/ /sdig pa'i las can 'chi bas 'jigs 'gyur te/ /chu chen
36b3(mdo 'grel): nang du gru ngan zhig pa bzhin/ /bsod nams byas shing sdig pa ma byas la/ /dam pa rnams kyi sngon gyi chos spyad pa/ /de ni nam yang 'chi bas 'jigs med de/ /brtan pa'i gru yis pha rol 'gro ba bzhin/ /sdig pa'i tshoms te nyi shu
36b4(mdo 'grel): rtsa brgyad pa'o/ //ji srid nyi ma ma shar ba/ /de srid srin bu me khyer snang/ /nyi ma shar bar gyur pa na/ /snang ba med cing sngon por 'gyur/ /ji srid de bzhin gshegs ma shar/ /de srid rtog ge ba rnams snang/ /'jig
36b5(mdo 'grel): rten rdzogs sangs rgyas shar ba/ /rtogs can nyan thos bcas mi snang/ /gces min gces par blos 'dzin cing/ /gces la gces par mi rtog pa/ /log par kun rtog spyod yul can/ /des ni gces pa thob mi 'gyur/ /
36b6(mdo 'grel): gces pa min la gces min dang/ /gces la gces par 'du shes pa/ /legs pa kun rtog spyod yul can/ /des ni gces pa thob par 'gyur/ /'di na lta dang nya la la mngon zhen pa'i/ /tshangs ma gsar dang gsar du 'phel
36b7(mdo 'grel): bdag /'khor bar rgyug cing 'gro dang sdod 'gyur te/ me nang lhung ba'i phye ma leb dang 'dra/ /'di la myong 'gyur gzhan la mi 'gyur ba 'am/ /'di ni the tshom tha dad ji snyed pa/ /de dag tshangs par spyad spyod 'bad pa dang/ /sems
37a1(mdo 'grel): par byed pas rab tu rnam par spong/ /gang zhig snyigs ma yod bzhin du/ /ngur smrig gos ni gyon byed pa/ /dul dang nges pa med pa dang/ /ngur smrig gyon pa'i 'os ma yin/ /gang zhig snyigs ma rnams spangs nas/ /tshul
37a2(mdo 'grel): khrims legs par mnyam gzhag pa/ /dul dang nges par ldan pa de/ /ngur smrig gyon pa'i 'os yin no/ /g.yo sgyu 'jungs dang ldan pa'i mi/ /kha dog dang ni gzugs ldan pa'am/ /yang na smra bar byed tsam gyis/ /pho mchog yin

37a5(mdo 'grel): khong pa rab gdug phyi rol 'phags tshul gyis/ /'jig rten 'di na 'khor dang bcas par rgyu/ /gang zhig rde 'gengs gnyid ni log pa dang/ /nyin dang mtshan du 'gre ldog nyal byed pa/ /rdzab nang phag chen lus rgyas ji lta bar/

37a7(mdo 'grel): bsdams shing/ /zas kyi tshong ni mi shes la/ /dran pa nyams dang le lo can/ /gtsang ma lta zhing gnas byed pa/ /de ni 'dod chags rnams kyis bcom/ /rlung gis mi brtan ljon shing bzhin/ /gang zhig dbang po legs bsdams
37b1(mdo 'grel): shing/ /zas kyi tshod ni shes pa dang/ /so sor dran zhing brtson 'grus ldan/ /mi gtsang lta bas gnas byed pa/ /de ni 'dod chags kyis mi choms/ /rlung gis ri bo mi g.yo bzhin/ /dgon par dga' ba bya 'os pa/ /de la skye bo mi dga' yang
37b2(mdo 'grel): nga la 'dod chags bral ba dga' / /'dod pa tshol bar byed rnams min/ /dgon pa 'am yang na grong dag gam/ /gshong ngam thang du dag kyang rung/ gang na 'phags pa bzhugs pa yi/ /sa de yid du 'ong ba yin/ /dam pa ring nas snang

41a5(mdo 'grel): khur por na ni bde bar 'gyur/ /lci ba'i khur dag nges bor na/ /phyi nas gzhan dag len mi 'gyur/ /kun sbyor thams cad zad bya'i phyir/ /sred pa thams cad rab tu spongs/ /phung po thams cad yongs shes na/ /srid pa phyi mar 'gro
41a6(mdo 'grel): ba med/ /don rnams bkrun pa la ni grogs ldan bde/ /srog dag rab tu gtugs la bsod nams bde/ /ngan don tsam gyis nges par chog shes bde/ /sdug bsngal thams cad nges par nub na bde/ /'di na me ni 'bar ba la/ /lcags
41a7(mdo 'grel): kyi tho bas brgyab pa yi/ /rim gyis nye bar zhi 'gyur te/ /ji ltar song ba mi shes pa ltar/ /'dod pa'i 'dam rdzab chu brgal cing/ /go 'phang mi g.yo thob pa dang/ /legs par rnam par grol rnams kyis/ /'gro ba gdags su med pa
41b1(mdo 'grel): yin/ gang zhig khong na 'khrug pa med pa dang/ /gang zhig srid dang srid min las log pa/ /de ni 'jigs bral bde zhing mya ngan med/ /lhas kyang lta zhing bsam du med par 'gyur/ /'di na gang dag chos mang thos pa dang/ /rtogs shing ci yang med pa kye re bde
41b2(mdo 'grel): skye bo skye bo'i sems la rab chags shing/ /cung zad yod pas brlag par 'gyur la ltos/ /'di na gang dag chos mang thos pa dang/ /rtogs shing ci yang med pa kye re bde/ /skye bo skye bo'i lus la rab chags shing/ /cung zad yod pa brlag par 'gyur la
41b3(mdo 'grel): ltos/ /skye bo ci med yon tan rtogs pa dang/ /skye bo ci yang med par 'gyur ba bde/ /skye bo skye bo'i sems la rab chags shing/ /cung zad yod pa brlag par 'gyur la ltos/ /skye bo ci med yon tan rtogs pa dang/ /skye bo ci yang med par 'gyur ba
41b4(mdo 'grel): bde/ /skye bo ci yang med par rab chags shing/ /cung zad yod pa brlag par 'gyur la ltos/ /gzhan gyi dbang gyur kun sdug ste/ /rang dbang yod pa thams cad bde/ /sbyor ba shin tu spang dka' ba/ /thun mong gyur pas brlag par zad/ /zhen par
41b5(mdo 'grel): gyur pa'i mi nang na/ /zhen pa med par gnas pa dang/ /zhen pa'i nang na ma zhen pa/ /kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/ /nad kyis thebs pa'i mi nang na/ /nad med par ni gnas pa dang/ /nad pa'i nang na nad med pa/ /kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/ /
41b6(mdo 'grel): 'tsho ba can gyi mi nad na/ /'tshe ba med par gnas pa dang/ /'tsho ba'i nad na 'tshe med par/ /kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/ /gnod sems can gyi mi nang na/ /gnod sems med par gnas pa dang/ /gnod sems can nad gnod med pa/ /
41b7(mdo 'grel): kye ma'o shin tu bde bar mtsho/ /sha khon can gyi mi nang ni/ /sha khon med par gnas pa dang/ /sha khon can nad khon med pa/ /kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/ /mi thi la dag rab bsregs kyang/ /nga la ci yang tshig pa med/ /nga la gang dag ci med
42a1(mdo 'grel): pas/ kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/ /nga la ci yang med mod kyi/ /dga' ba zad par byed pas na/ /'od gsal gyi ni lha bzhin du/ /kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/ /'jig tshogs la ni mi rten pas/ /nga la ci yang med mod kyi/ /dga' ba
42a2(mdo 'grel): zad par byed pas na/ /kye ma'o shin tu bde bar 'tsho/ /len pa'i rkyen gyis phrad cing reg 'gyur gyi/ /len pa med dang phrad cing reg med pas/ /bdag dang gzhan gyis bskyed pa'i bde sdug gis/ /dgon pa 'am grong du reg par mi 'gyur ro/ /
42a3(mdo 'grel): 'jig rten 'di na bde dang sdug bsngal gyis/ /skyes bu dam pa mtho dman mi 'byung zhing/ /brtan rnams 'dod pa'i rgyu yis mi 'khyal bar/ /skyes bu dam pa kun tu 'gro bar byed/ /bde ba'i tshoms te sum cu ba'o// //ched du
42a4(mdo 'grel): brjod pa'i tshoms/ /bam po bzhi pa ste tha ma/ /gzung bar dka' zhing yang ba dang/ /gang du dga' bar 'gro ba yi/ /sems dul ba ni legs pa ste/ /sems dul ba yis bde ba 'dren/ /bdud kyi gzhi dag spong ba na/ /chu bo'i gnas
42a5(mdo 'grel): nas rab gton te/ /thang la song ba'i nya lta bur/ /bdag gi sems ni yongs su g.yo/ /nyi ma las ni 'od zer ltar/ /bdag gi sems ni so sor rgyug /de dag mkhas pas nges bzlog ste/ /lcags kyu yis ni glang chen bzhin/ /ngal
42a6(mdo 'grel): ba don med spyod pa dang/ /bltar med snying po med pa de/ /rtag tu gdul bar bya ba'i phyir/ /sems de la ni nga smra'o/ /sems 'di sngon chad ji ltar 'dod pa dang/ /dga' 'gyur spyod cing rgyu bar byed pa dang/ /glang chen myos la mi yi
42a7(mdo 'grel): lcags kyu ltar/ /da ni tshul bzhin bya bas de gzung ngo/ /khang khyim byed pa de yis ni/ /yang yang skye ba'i sdug bsngal can/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba du ma zhig /da ltar phan chad khyod kyis phyung/ /khang khyim byed pa khyod mthong bas/ /
42b1(mdo 'grel): khyim gyi gdung chen rnams bcom pa/ /phyam rnams thams cad bcag nas su/ /phyin chad khyim med mi gzhug go /sems ni 'du byed dang bral nas/ /'di nyid la ni zad par 'dod/ /sems ni g.yo zhing brdzun pa ste/ /ring du 'gro zhing bzlog dka' ba/ mnga' 
42b2(mdo 'grel): mkhan me yis spong ba ltar/ /yid gzhungs pa yis bsrang bar bya/ /gang zhig lus med phug na gnas/ /gcig pu rgyu zhing ring 'gro ba'i/ /sems de dul bar byed pa ni/ /'jigs pa che las thar bar 'gyur/ /log pa'i smon ldan sems gang gis/
42b3(mdo 'grel): bdag nyid sdug bsngal byed 'gyur ba/ /de ltar khon gyis khon can dang/ /dgra bos dgra la byed mi 'gyur/ /gang dag smon gang sems ldan gyis/ /bdag nyid bde bar byed 'gyur ba/ /de ltar pha dang ma dag dang/ /gnyen gzhan gyis kyang byed mi 'gyur//
42b4(mdo 'grel): ji ltar khang steng g.yog nyes na/ /char pa yongs su 'dzag pa ltar/ /de bzhin sems ni ma bsgoms pa/ /'dod chags rnams kyis yongs su bcom/ /ji ltar khang stengs g.yog legs na/ /char pa rnam par mi 'dzag pa/ /de bzhin legs
42b5(mdo 'grel): par bsgoms pa'i sems/ /'dod chags rnams kyis yongs mi tshoms/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog nyes na/ /char pa yongs su 'dzag pa ltar/ /de bzhin sems ni ma bsgoms pa/ /zhe sdang rnams kyis yongs su bcom/ /ji ltar khang
42b6(mdo 'grel): steng g.yog legs na/ /char pa rnam par mi 'dzag pa/ /de bzhin legs par bsgoms pa'i sems/ /zhe sdang rnams kyis yongs mi tshoms/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog nyes na/ /char pa yongs su 'dzag pa ltar/ /de bzhin sems ni ma
42b7(mdo 'grel): bsgoms pa/ /gti mug rnams kyis yongs su bcom/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog legs na/ /char pa rnam par mi 'dzag pa/ /de bzhin legs par bsgoms pa'i sems/ /gti mug rnams kyis yongs/ /mi tshoms/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog
43a1(mdo 'grel): nyes na/ char pa yongs su 'dzag pa ltar/ /de bzhin sems ni ma bsgoms pa/ /nga rgyal rnams kyis yongs su bcom/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog legs na/ /char pa rnam par mi 'dzag pa/ /de bzhin legs par bsgoms pa'i
43a2(mdo 'grel): sems/ /nga rgyal rnams kyis yongs mi choms/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog nyes na/ /char pa yongs su 'dzag pa ltar/ /de bzhin sems ni ma bsgoms pa/ /chags pa rnams kyis yongs su bcom/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog legs na/ /

43a4(mdo 'grel): rnams kyis yongs su bcom/ /ji ltar khang steng g.yog legs na/ /char pa rnam par mi 'dzag pa/ /de bzhin legs par bsgoms pa'i sems/ /sred pa rnams kyis yongs mi choms/ /chos kyi sngon du yid 'gro ste/ /yid mgyogs
43a5(mdo 'grel): yid ni gtso bo yin/ /gal te yid rab gdug pa yis/ /smras sam yang na byas kyang rung/ /de yis de ni sdug bsngal 'thob/ /'khor los mgo bo bcad pa bzhin/ /chos kyi sngon du yid 'gro ste/ /yid 'gyogs yid ni gtso bo yin/ /gal
43a6(mdo 'grel): te yid rab dad pa yis/ /smras sam yang na byas kyang rung/ /de yi de ni sdug bsngal 'thob/ /grib ma rjes su 'brang ba bzhin/ /rtsod pa ched cher 'dzin pa dang/ /sems ni nyon mongs gyur pa yis/ /glags skabs tshol bar byed pa yis/ /legs
43a7(mdo 'grel): bshad legs par mi shes so/ /sdang ba 'am yang na 'khrug pa 'am/ /ngang pa med pa'i sems dag gis/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa yi/ /dam chos kun shes mi nus so/ /gang gis bag med sems dang ni/ /khro ba rnam par btul ba dang//
43b1(mdo 'grel): 'di na gnod sems rab spangs pa/ /des ni legs par bshad pa shes/ /sems kyi brtan pa med pa yis/ /dam chos rnam par shes mi 'gyur/ /ngang pa 'gyur ldog byed pa yis/ /shes rab yongs su rdzogs mi 'gyur/ /kun rtogs la 'chums brten
43b2(mdo 'grel): pa yis/ /lta ngan sum cu rtsa drug gis/ /chu yi rgyun ni gang yin pa/ /yid kyi rgyun las rab tu 'bab/ /dga' sems dbang po phal pa dang/ /sems kyi rjes 'brang zhan pa yi/ /mi de'i grags 'grib 'bras lhags pa'i/ /ljon shing la ni bya bzhin no//
43b3(mdo 'grel): sems khyod phung khrol 'dod la dga' mi byed/ /brtson sems bag yod pa la gnas par gyis/ /bag med byas pas dmyal bar bcos pa na/ /lcags gong ming pas khyod ni ma du shig /ldang ba'i dus tshe 'dug par byed pa dang/ /lang tsho stobs
43b4(mdo 'grel): ldan mi 'thad khyim 'dug dang/ /bsam pa rdzogs tshe le lo byed pa yi/ /mi yis shes rab lam rtogs mi 'gyur ro/ /phran tshegs rnam rtog zhib mor rnam rtog pas/ /nad na gnas pa'i yid ni g.yon par spyo/ /yid kyi rnam rtog de dag ma
43b5(mdo 'grel): shes na/ /'khrul sems yang dang yang du rgyug par byed/ /gang zhig dran ldan rnam 'byed brtson pa dang/ /rnam par rtog la mkhas pas de shes na/ /nad na gnas pa'i yid ni g.yen spyo ba/ /thams cad ma lus blo yis rab tu spong/ /lus ni bum
43b6(mdo 'grel): pa 'dra bar rtogs byas shing/ /grong khyer 'dra ba'i sems kyis sran btsugs nas/ /shes rab mtshon gyis bdud dang g.yul sprad de/ /btul nas gnas med par ni bsrung bar bya/ /'jig rten 'di dag bum pa 'drar rtogs shing/ /de
43b7(mdo 'grel): bzhin chos rnams smig rgyu 'drar shes nas/ /shes rab mtshon gyi bdud dang g.yul sprad de/ /btul nas gnas med par ni bsrung bar bya/ /lus 'di dbu ba 'dra bar rtogs byas shing/ /grong khyer 'dra ba'i sems kyis sran btsugs
44a1(mdo 'grel): nas/ shes rab mtshon gyis bdud dang g.yul sprad de/ /btul nas gnas med par ni bsrung bar bya/ /'jig rten 'di dag dbu ba 'drar rtogs shing/ /grong khyer 'dra ba'i sems kyis sran btsugs nas/ /shes rab mtshon gyis bdud
44a2(mdo 'grel): dang g.yul sprad de/ /btul nas gnas med par ni bsrung bar bya/ /gang gis byang chub yan lag bdun/ /sems kyis logs par bsgoms pa dang/ /gang zhig len la mi dga' zhing/ /len pa rab tu spangs pa dang/ /zag zad skyon rnams bsal
44a3(mdo 'grel): ba bde/ /'jig rten dag na mya ngan 'das/ /gang zhig g.yog rnga'i rtse mo ltar/ /rang gi sems ni rjes bsrung zhing/ /'byung po rnams la brtser ldan pa/ /de yi bde ba yod mi nyams/ /gang phyir glang po'i glang po che/ /mche ba bzang po'i glang
44a4(mdo 'grel): chen dang/ /sems dang sems ni mnyam pas na/ /de phyir gcig pu gnas su dgyes/ /gang zhig yid la gnos byed cing/ /'byung po kun la brtse ba dang/ /'byung po rnams la byams byed pa/ /de ni nams kyang khon mi 'byung/ /gang la
44a5(mdo 'grel): gnod pa'i sems med cing/ /'byung po kun la brtse ba dang/ /srog chags kun la byams byed pa/ /de la gnas kyang khon mi 'byung/ /gang la gnod pa'i sems med cing/ /'byung po rnams la brtse ba dang/ /sems can kun la byams byed pa/
44a6(mdo 'grel): de la nams kyang khon mi 'byung/ /mdza' bshes kun dang grogs kun dang/ /'byung po kun la brtse ba dang/ /byams pa'i sems ni bsgoms byas na/ /bde ba shin tu 'phel bar 'gyur/ /gal te gang zhig srog chags 'ga' la'ang sdang

44b1(mdo 'grel): yid kyis su/ /dge ba'i chos la sgom byed pa/ /grub pa dang ni bde ba 'thob/ /yang dag shes pas rnam grol zhing/ /skyob pa nye bar zhi 'gyur ba/ /de yi yid ni zhi 'gyur zhing/ /lus dang ngag gi las kyang zhi/ /ji ltar rtse gcig sems kyis ni/ /chos rnams

44b3(mdo 'grel): la dga' ba/ /de dag 'dod pa rtse mi byed/ /gang zhig cung zad gdung med pa'i/ /thub pa kye ma'o dga' bar 'gyur/ /gang gi sems ni brag lta bur/ /rab tu g.yo ba med 'dug pa/ /chags pa'i gnas la mi chags te/ /khro ba'i gnas la khro med par/
44b4(mdo 'grel): gang yid de ltar gyur pa de/ /sdug bsngal thob par ga la 'gyur/ /skur pa mi gang? pa gnod mi bya/ /so sor thar pas bsdam par bya/ /zas kyi tshod kyang shes par bya/ /bas mdza' dgon par gnas bya zhing/ /lhag pa'i sems la rnal 'byor bya/ /'di

45b1(mdo 'grel): pa'i tshig de thos gyur kyang/ /dge slong yid legs gzhag la ji mi snyam/ /g.yul dor glang chen mda' yis bsnun pa bzhin/ /bzo yis mi 'tsho yang zhing bdag la dga' / /dbang po dul dang kun las rnam grol zhing/ /khyim la ma chags bdag
45b2(mdo 'grel): med 'dod sred spangs/ /gcig pu spyod byed de ni dge slong yin/ /'tsho gtsang snyom las med pa yi/ /grogs po mthun pa bsten bya zhing/ /so so bgo bsha' bya ba dang/ /spyod yul cho ga mkhas par bya/ /spyod yul cho ga mkhas pa yis/ /

46a3(mdo 'grel): grong ba'i chos ni 'dzin byed pa/ /cig dge slong min pa snyam/ /gang zhig dge dang sdig pa dag /rab spangs tshangs par spyod ldan zhing/ /sde tshogs spangs nas spyod byed ltar/ /de ni dge slong zhes brjod do/ /dge slong gang zhig byams gnas shing

46a5(mdo 'grel): 'gyur/ /dge slong gang zhig byams gnas shing/ /sangs rgyas bstan la rab dad pas/ /des ni kun sbyor kun zad pa/ /rim gyis mngon sum byed par 'gyur/ /dge slong gang zhig byams gnas shing/ /sangs rgyas bstan la rab dad pas/ /
46a6(mdo 'grel): bdag nyid ngan 'gro las 'dren te/ /'dam rdzab las ni glang chen bzhin/ /dge slong gang zhig byams gnas shing/ /sangs rgyas bstan la rab dad pas/ /sdig pa'i chos rnams sdug byed de/ /rlung gis ljon shing lo ma bzhin/ /dge
46a7(mdo 'grel): slong gang zhig byams gnas shing/ /sangs rgyas bstan la rab dad pas/ /mya ngan 'das dang nye ba'i phyir/ /yongs su nyams 'gyur mi srid do/ /sems dga' yid ni bzang ba dang/ /dga' dang mi dga' zil gnon pa'i/ /
46b1(mdo 'grel): dge slong dga' ba myong ba yis/ /sdug bsngal zad pa thob par 'gyur/ /lus zhi dag ni zhi ba dang/ /sems zhi legs par mnyam bzhag cing/ /'jig rten zang zing spangs pa yi/ /dge slong nyer zhi yin zhes brjod/ /ting 'dzin med la shes nga ba med/
46b2(mdo 'grel): shes rab med la ting 'dzin med/ /shes rab ting 'dzin ldan pa dang/ /dge slong yin zhes brjod par bya/ /ting 'dzin med la shes rab med/ /shes rab med la ting 'dzin med/ /shes rab ting 'dzin ldan pa de/ /mya ngan 'das dang nye ba nyid
46b3(mdo 'grel): de bas ting 'dzin shes rab la/ /mkhas pa rnams kyis 'jug bya ste/ /de bzhin shes rab dge slong de'i/ /dang por bya ba 'di yin no/ /dge slong yang dag sdom spyod pas/ /chog shes dbang po bsdams par bya/ /so sor thar pas bsdoms par bya//
46b4(mdo 'grel): zas kyi tshod kyang shes par bya/ /bas mdza' i dgon par gnas pa dang/ /lhag pa'i sems la rnal 'byor bya/ /'di ni sangs rgyas bstan pa yin/ /gang gi lus dang ngag dang ni/ /yid la nyes byas med gyur pa/ /de ni dag pa'i tshul khrims can/ /
46b5(mdo 'grel): ngo tsha'i yid ldan dge slong yin/ /gang gis rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi/ /phyogs kyi chos bdun legs bsgoms pa/ /de ni dge ba'i chos can de/ /mnyam gzhag dge slong yin zhes gsungs/ /'di na gang zhig bdag nyid kyi/ /sdug bsngal zad par
46b6(mdo 'grel): rab shes la/ /dge zhing shes ldan pa de/ /zag med dge slong yin zhes gsungs/ /zag pa zad pa ma thob na/ /tshul khrims brtul zhugs tsam dag gam/ /yang na thos pa mang po 'am/ /dben pa dag tu gnas kyang rung/ /ting 'dzin thob
46b7(mdo 'grel): par gyur kyang ngal/ /? drod tshong pa'i dge slong min/ /phung po la ni bdag zer ba'i/ /'jig rten 'di dag gdung ba ste/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub bde ba ni/ /'phags pas bsten pa mngon du bya/ /ji lta ji ltar bsam byas pas/ /de lta de ltar
47a1(mdo 'grel): gzhag du 'gyur/ /gzhan du gyur pa'i 'jig rten 'di/ /srid pa la chags srid la dga' / /srid pa mngon chags srid pa lta/ /srid pa nyid la mngon par dga' / /dga' bya gang yin de sdug bsngal/ /kyi g.ya' gang yin de bde bas/ /
47a2(mdo 'grel): srid pa rab tu spang ba'i phyir/ /'di na tshangs pa spyod pa bsten/ /dge spyod bram ze ji snyed pa/ /srid pas srid las nges 'byung zer/ /de dag thams cad srid pa las/ /nges 'byung mi shes brjod par bya/ /dge sbong bram ze ji snyed pa/ /srid pas
47a3(mdo 'grel): srid la nges 'byung zer/ /de dag thams cad srid pa las/ /rnam grol min zhes brjod par bya/ /len pa'i rkyen gyi sdug bsngal byung/ /sdug bsngal las ni len pa byung/ /len pa thams cad yongs zad na/ /sdug bsngal rab tu byung ba med/
47a4(mdo 'grel): thams cad na srid pa'i rnam pa ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad ni mi rtag pa sdug bsngal ba yongs su 'gyur ba'i chos can yin no zhes de ltar de dag la yang dag par shes rab kyis ji lta ba bzhin du mthong na srid pa'i sred pa rab tu spong bar 'gyur zhing
47a5(mdo 'grel): srid pa med pas mngon par dga' bar 'gyur/ /de ltar mya ngan las 'das pa'i dge slong slob pa ni gzhan du len pa med cing yang srid pa med par 'gyur te/ /bdud zil gyis gnon pa dang/ /g.yul las rgyal ba dang/ srid pa thams cad
47a6(mdo 'grel): las rab tu 'das pa 'di lta bu 'di ni sdug bsngal gyi mdza' yin no/ /dge slong dngos po bcad pa dang/ /nye bar zhi zhing sems zhi ba/ /de ni yang srid med par 'gyur/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rnam par spangs/ /dge slong dngos po bcad pa dang/ nye bar
47a7(mdo 'grel): zhi zhing sems zhi ba/ /de ni bdud kyi 'ching bas grol/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rnam par spangs/ /dge slong dngos po bcad pa dang/ /sems ni zag pa med gyur pa/ /de ni yang srid med pa ste/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rnam par spangs/ /dge slong dngos po bcad pa
47b1(mdo 'grel): dang/ sems ni zag pa med gyur pa/ /de ni bdud kyi 'ching las grol/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rnam par spangs/ /dge slong dngos po bcad pa dang/ /srid pa'i sred pa gtubs gyur pa/ /de ni yang srid med par 'gyur/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rnam par spangs/ /dge slong dngos po
47b2(mdo 'grel): bcad pa dang/ /srid pa sred pa bcad gyur pa/ /de ni bdud kyi 'ching las grol/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rnam par spangs/ /gang zhig 'dam rdzab legs brgal cing/ /grong gi tsher ma dkrugs pa dang/ /'dod chags zad pa rjes thob pa/ /de ni dag slong yin zhes

47b6(mdo 'grel): 'ching dang grong gi tsher ma thub pa dang/ /gang zhig ri bo bzhin gnas mi bkri zhing/ /sdug nges mi g.yos 'di ni dge slong yin/ /skur pa mi 'debs sgro 'dogs mi byed cing/ /'jig rten 'di kun brdzun rtogs dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol min pa'i
47b7(mdo 'grel): pha rol pa/ /srong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rdzeb bzhin/ /sbrul gyis dug btang ba la sman bzhin du/ /'dod chags langs pa 'dul ba'i dge slong gang/ /de ni pha rol min pa'i pha rol po/ /spong ste sbrul rgas lpags rnying rje ba bzhin/ /sbrul gyis dug
